Currently, Red Dysentery, Typhoid Fever, and Severe Plague Have Been Discovered in Yuanwu; The Transmission Is Extremely Severe, and Fifty to Sixty People Die Daily; If Prevention and Control Measures Are Not Taken, What Harm Can Be Imagined? In addition to Writing to the County Government to Order the Public Security Bureau to Take Appropriate Precautions, We Sincerely Request Your Association to Send Personnel with Medicine to Yuanwu for Diagnosis and Treatment to Help the People, Which Would Be a Great Kindness; (5) A Report from Wang Shao Yi, Chairman of the Shangqiu Relief Association, States: After the Disaster Relief in Shangqiu, the People's Hardship Has Not Recovered; Fortunately, This Year's Wheat Harvest Was Good, and There Is Hope for Autumn; We Thought We Could Rest a Little, But Unexpectedly, the Epidemic Broke Out; People Often Die Without Medical Treatment; According to Investigations, Thirty-Eight People Died Recently at the Train Station, Twenty-Four Died in Beiguan, Nine Died in Dongguan, and Deaths Are Also Common in the City and the Southwest Two Gates; In the Wuzhang and Liulin Areas of the Sixth District, More Than One Hundred People Died; The Symptoms Include Severe Vomiting and Diarrhea, or No Vomiting and Diarrhea, or Vomiting, Diarrhea, and Cramps; The Area Is Remote, and Medical Treatment and Medicine Are Lacking; We Are Truly Afraid of Delaying People's Lives; In addition to Working with the County Government to Promote Hygiene and Make Every Effort to Prevent and Control the Situation, We Urgently Request Your Examination and Approval and the Swift Issuance of a Large Amount of Epidemic Prevention Medicine for Relief Purposes, Which Would Be in the Public Interest; (6) The Provincial Relief Association Received a Telegram from Zhao Minle, County Magistrate of Wen County, Stating: The Epidemic Situation in Wen County Is Particularly Severe, and a Prevention and Medical Treatment Center Has Been Established to Work Hard on Prevention and Control, and Epidemic Prevention Campaigns Have Been Conducted; However, There Is Much Disease and Little Medicine, Which Is Truly Insufficient; According to Doctors and Patients, Ten Drops of Water Is Miraculously Effective; We Request Your Association to Swiftly Send Personnel with a Large Batch of Medicine to Save the People from Death; (7) Liu Xiaoyu, County Magistrate of She County, Reports: The Counties Under My Jurisdiction Have Suffered From Years of Banditry, Drought, Hail, and Epidemics, and the People Are Extremely Distressed; Although the Spring and Autumn Seedlings Have Been Widely Planted, Unexpectedly, on the Twenty-Seventh and Twenty-Ninth Days of the Fifth Month of the Lunar Calendar This Year, There Were Thunderstorms, Strong Winds, and Violent Hail, as Large as Fists and as Small as Eggs; It Lasted for Several Hours; The Ground Was Covered with Six Inches of Ice, and the Ditches Were Several Feet Deep; In Areas Such as the Eastern Defense of the Sha River, the Crops Were Destroyed, the Leaves Were All Fallen, and Many People and Animals Were Injured; The Accumulated Hail Did Not Melt for Two Days; Refugees Were Everywhere; The Sight Was Heartbreaking; The People Have No Way to Survive; We Sincerely Fear That They Will Resort to Desperate Measures; We Urgently Request Special Consideration and Generous Relief, Which Would Be in the Public Interest.

Thorough Investigation of Corruption in Anhui Northern Relief Efforts

Bengbu Circles Organize Support Association

Bengbu Correspondence: The case of Quan Shaowu, Anhui Northern Relief Commissioner, and Chang Shucheng, owner of Baoxing Flour Mill and director of relief wheat transportation, engaging in private gain and corrupt practices, delaying relief efforts, has recently been investigated by a delegation organized by Sun Yunxin and Wang Chusheng, representatives of the National Government Disaster Relief Committee, Lu Yinan and Yue Xiangru, representatives of the Anhui Shanghai Fellow-Townsmen Association, and Shi Dechun and Wang Zhaoquan, representatives of the Anhui Beijing Fellow-Townsmen Association, and other six people. They have been conducting thorough investigations into the truth of the corrupt practices and auditing relief books and receipts and collecting evidence of private gain. Representatives from local circles here have also organized a Bengbu Thorough Investigation Support Association, and Peng Zhuoru and eight others have been elected as members. The association has now been established and today (30th) issued official letters notifying the relief branches in the twenty-one counties of northern Anhui. The original letter stated, "Dear Sirs, Unfortunately, northern Anhui suffered a flood disaster, the Huai River flooded, fields and houses were submerged, and refugees were everywhere. Fortunately, our National Government and Anhui fellow-townsmen, taking on the spirit of 'drowning as if they themselves were drowning' and 'hunger as if they themselves were hungry', widely bestowed relief to save millions of affected fellow countrymen. There is much to admire in disaster relief and helping the distressed. However, due to the wide scope and difficult supervision, and the complexity of distribution, there were inevitably errors. Therefore, the central government sent several investigation teams to investigate the relief in northern Anhui, but they were ultimately unable to conduct a thorough investigation. Now, another thorough investigation team has come to Bengbu, and our association, in order to assist the investigation team in thoroughly investigating the malpractices in relief efforts, and to contribute our opinions to the investigation team, has organized the Bengbu Thorough Investigation Support Association. However, we are short-sighted and unskilled, and our knowledge is limited. Therefore, we request that your association, within three days of receiving this letter, inform us in detail of the quantity of relief wheat, funds, and flour that should have been received, the amount received, the amount distributed, and the amount remaining for official relief, charity relief, industrial relief, and emergency relief, so that we can compile a complete statistic, so that the relief efforts in northern Anhui can be clarified one day. We are notifying your association accordingly, and we hope to receive a reply. We would be most grateful." (July 30th)

Divided into Five Groups to Inspect Qingdao

Wang's Speech: The reporter visited Mr. Wang Xiaolai this morning to inquire about the situation of the anti-war movement. Mr. Wang made the following remarks: "We feel that since the September 18th Incident and the January 28th Incident, the Japanese have committed atrocities in the Northeast and Shanghai, and the people have suffered untold misery. In order to save the people from suffering, we must unite against foreign aggression and should not have any more civil wars. Now the national economy is in dire straits, and the raw materials used by industry and commerce are completely dependent on foreigners. Industry and commerce are like newborn babies. The raw materials from abroad are like a knife. If the baby is repeatedly cut by the knife, how can we expect it to grow? Therefore, if we want to develop industry and commerce, we must first seek the ability to produce raw materials ourselves, so as to avoid the baby being cut by the knife. Our country has been in civil war for many years, which has had a major impact on the local and national economy. Economic panic and construction are out of the question. Civil war and construction are closely related. If we want to build, we must first abolish civil war before we can hope to succeed. We have launched a movement to abolish civil war, and some people outside are quite skeptical. But what is called civil war is very easy to distinguish. Fighting for power and seizing territory are all civil wars. As for the Red bandits who kill and set fires, we should find ways to eliminate them, which cannot be counted as civil war. We sent people to Guangdong to persuade them about the recent incidents, and the results were good. In short, we will never cooperate with any civil war that is detrimental to the local area or the country. Only, one more person in this movement has the strength of one person, and we urgently hope that local people's groups will participate in joint cooperation to facilitate progress. Therefore, we take this opportunity to contact various places. Now this conference is scheduled to be held in Shanghai on August 27, when we can discuss the measures together," etc. (July 29)

Jiangxi Circles Oppose Production and Sales Tax

Tax Collection Increases Prices, Affecting the Livelihood of Ordinary People

Businessmen and Merchants Resolutely Request Cancellation

Nanchang Correspondence: The Jiangxi Provincial Government, due to the lack of funds for bandit suppression and post-disaster reconstruction, has added a production and sales tax on imports and exports, as reported in previous news. In addition to imported foreign goods, the goods subject to the tax include bamboo and wood, paper, ramie cloth, porcelain, medicinal materials, and soybeans produced in the province. Bureaus have been established in Jiujiang, Hukou, Nanchang, Zhangshu, Jingdezhen, and other places to collect the tax. The tax rate is based on the consumption tax of the former Special Commissioner's Office of the Ministry of Finance, divided into daily necessities, semi-luxury goods, and luxury goods, ranging from 2.5% to 10%. When the tax was first implemented, merchants and people in various places strongly opposed it. Industries in Nanchang and Zhangshu petitioned the provincial government, stating that the province had suffered from banditry and chaos, people's lives were difficult, and all industries were declining. The taxes collected on various goods would indirectly be borne by the people. In this time of saving the dying and healing the wounded, how could they further increase the burden on the people? However, Governor Xiong told the petitioners to endure the pain temporarily and to take responsibility for suppressing bandits and saving Jiangxi. The petitioners returned empty-handed. Later, the Nanchang and Zhangshu Chambers of Commerce prepared to launch a larger and more effective opposition. Governor Xiong stated that destroying the donation for bandit suppression and post-disaster reconstruction was tantamount to destroying bandit suppression, which was a lack of understanding of the greater good, and ordered the Public Security Bureau to strictly investigate and punish merchants who opposed the tax donation. The opponents in this city then disappeared. It is said that merchants and people in several places are still very determined in their opposition. For example, when the people sent by the General Bureau of Production and Sales Tax arrived, the merchants and people of the whole port blocked them from landing and agreed not to sell food to the people of the tax bureau, not to rent houses to the tax collectors, and hotels and inns were not allowed to let them rest. The intensity of the situation can be seen. Yesterday, a gentleman in the business community said that the government estimated to collect 2.5 million to 3 million yuan from this tax annually. However, Jiangxi Province has been ravaged by bandits for five or six years, the bandit areas account for 70% to 80%, and due to natural and man-made disasters, the rural economy has completely collapsed. The purchasing power of foreign goods has been declining like a river flowing down, and it is difficult to expect imported taxes to improve. On the export side, the producing areas of bamboo and wood are in Chongyi and Shangyou in southern Jiangxi, and Chongren and Yihuang in eastern Jiangxi, all of which are in the hands of bandits. The main producing areas of paper are Qianshan, Guangfeng, Yihuang, and Wanzai. Most of the raw materials are bamboo, and 80% to 90% of the mountainous areas with bamboo are occupied by bandits. Due to the impact of the September 18th Incident last year, the sales of ramie cloth have greatly decreased, and the coarse cloth sold to Korea has disappeared. Yudu, Ningdu, Wan'an, and Guangxin produce the most oil, which used to be a major export. Recently, these counties have been completely bandit-ridden, and oil from other provinces is imported from Hukou. Jingdezhen porcelain is a world-famous industry and a major product of China. In recent years, it has been under pressure from foreign porcelain and is on the verge of extinction. It was captured by bandits twice in the past two years, and its essence has been lost. Most of the businesses have not yet recovered. The prospect of export tax is also not difficult to imagine. Moreover, after the implementation of this tax donation, the cost of export goods has increased, and sales have been greatly affected. The price of imported goods has increased, such as white sugar, which used to be 600 copper coins per catty, has now risen to 720, and foreign oil, which used to sell for 520, is now more than 600. The prices of other goods have increased by 10% or 20%. The livelihood of ordinary people is unbearable. Therefore, Jiangxi fellow villagers abroad are unanimously opposed to it. Celebrities such as Li Xiehe, Liu Zhi, Xu Sudong, Zhang Dingfan, Zhou Lisheng, and Sun Jingya have also successively petitioned the central government to order the provincial government to immediately cancel the tax in order to relieve the suffering of the people. It is said that Minister Song has sent a telegram to the province asking Governor Xiong to cancel the production and sales tax that is a disguised form of Likin. The telegram has been published in newspapers in Beijing and Shanghai. However, it is still unknown when the bureaus will cancel this tax. (July 27)

Jiangsu Provincial Chamber of Commerce Sub-districts

Convenes Talks with Various Chambers of Commerce

Announces Assistance in Collecting Business Tax

Zhenjiang Correspondence: The executive and supervisory committee members of the Jiangsu Provincial Chamber of Commerce previously held a discussion on business tax rates and collection matters and decided on the following six points: (1) The original business tax rate of 1/1000 will be increased to 2/1000, the original rate of 2/1000 will be increased to 4/1000, and the original rates of 5/1000 and 10/1000 will remain unchanged. Wholesale businesses will still be taxed at half rate. (2)

The gold and silver industry will be treated as a manufacturing industry and will be taxed based on the amount of capital. (3) The business tax will be handled concurrently by the finance bureaus of each county. Counties without a finance bureau will be handled concurrently by the county government. (4) The quarterly tax payment will be collected in the first month of each quarter. If a shop closes midway, the tax can be refunded based on the date. (5) The collection matters will be assisted by one or two responsible persons recommended by the local chamber of commerce. (6) The Provincial Chamber of Commerce will notify the county-level chambers of commerce to encourage local shops to declare their business tax in accordance with regulations and will convene meetings in sub-districts based on the former prefectural areas to announce the intention to assist the provincial government in collecting the tax in order to facilitate implementation and achieve practical results. The Provincial Chamber of Commerce, based on the above resolution, will divide the districts according to the former prefectural areas and will convene representatives from each chamber of commerce on August 8th, asking the conveners of each district to choose a convenient location nearby to convene a meeting to discuss assistance measures. The following is a list of the sub-districts and conveners: Suzhou Prefecture: Wu County, Wujiang, Kunshan, Changshu, Shi Yunqing, Convener; Changzhou Prefecture: Wujin, Wuxi, Yixing, Jiangyin, Jingjiang, Qian Sunqing, Lin Junbao, Conveners; Songjiang Prefecture: Songjiang, Nanhui, Jinshan, Shanghai, Fengxian, Qingpu, Chuansha, Cai Zhongyu, Zhang Tianmin, Conveners; Taicang Prefecture: Taicang, Baoshan, Jiading, Qidong, Chongming, Cai Zhongyu, Zhang Tianmin, Conveners; Zhenjiang Prefecture: Zhenjiang, Danyang, Jiyang, Jintan, Yangzhou, Lu Xiaopo, Yu Xiaochuan, Hu Jianchun, Conveners; Jiangning Prefecture: Jurong, Luhe, Jiangning, Gaochun, Lishui, Jiangpu, Qingxuan, Convener; Xuzhou Prefecture: Tongshan, Feng County, Pei County, Xiao County, Dangshan, Pi County, Suqian, Suining, Lan Bohua, Convener; Huaian Prefecture: Huai

Local Correspondence

Songjiang

Change of Director of the County Hospital: Zhang Zhongji, Director of the County Songjiang Hospital, resigned from his position due to his age and the inability to expand due to limited funding. The County Government approved his resignation and appointed Zhang Shaozan, a famous doctor, to take over the position. He is scheduled to take over on the 5th. The new Director Zhang is currently the Director of the Epidemic Hospital.

Graduation of Tax Police Training Institute

The Ministry of Finance Tax Police Officer Training Institute held the graduation ceremony for the second class of students yesterday. Wu Shangzhi, representative of the Director-General, and Lu Gujian attended the ceremony and delivered training speeches. Zhang Bingyuan, Standing Committee Member of the County Party Department, and representatives from various agencies attended the grand ceremony. Director Yao Guanshun reported on the training process and economic situation. Afterwards, student representative Yu Rilong gave a reply. After speeches by the guests, Director Yao, together with the representative of the Director-General, issued graduation certificates. There were twenty-two graduating students, including Zhong Shisan, etc. Liu Qu'e was the best in the total score and practical subjects, and Bao Yi was the best student. Special awards were given. There was a Peking opera performance in the evening. The graduation ceremony was a grand event for a time.

Suzhou

Sentence Announced in the Liyang Land Tax Embezzlement Case

The appeal case of Zheng Chengyuan, Magistrate of Liyang County, et al., for land tax embezzlement was sentenced yesterday (1st) morning by Zheng Zhiguo, a judge of the First Criminal Division of the Suzhou Higher Court. Except for Zheng et al., who were released on bail and did not appear, Huang Xing'an, Cao Qingzhi, and Shen Zhiqing, who were in custody, were ordered to be brought to the court. Judge Zheng stood up and announced the main text of the judgment. The original judgment was revoked except for the portions concerning Shi Taoyong, Shi Qinglian, Hu Jinghua, and confiscation. Huang Xing'an was sentenced to four years of imprisonment for jointly and continuously embezzling items held in public office, and fined 2,000 yuan, and deprived of civil rights for eight years. Shen Zhiqing, Lu Zhiwen, and Zhao Dianhua were each sentenced to two years of imprisonment for jointly and continuously embezzling items held in public office, and fined 1,000 yuan, and deprived of civil rights for four years. Zheng Chengyuan was sentenced to four years of imprisonment for accepting bribes for actions that violated his duties, and fined 2,000 yuan, and deprived of civil rights for eight years. Ren Shuchun was sentenced to two months of imprisonment for the crime of joint intimidation. Di Hongxun was sentenced to one year of imprisonment for the crime of joint intimidation. Cao Qingzhi was acquitted of the charge of paying bribes, and the remaining charges were acquitted. Zhou Shi was acquitted. Pan Bin's public prosecution was not accepted. The other appeals were rejected. Huang Xing'an and Shen Zhiqing were returned to custody. Cao Qingzhi was released on bail with a bail bond of 400 yuan.

Wujiang

New Trial Judge Arrives in the County to Take Office

Shen Shouchun, the trial judge of this county, has been dismissed by the High Court and has been replaced by Xu Jichang. He arrived in the county from Suzhou yesterday and is scheduled to take office on August 1.

The Kidnapped Victim in Wubuli Has Been Rescued

Xiangyun, the grandson-in-law of the elderly Mrs. Lin of Wubuli Village outside the North Gate of the city, was kidnapped by bandits. His family delayed in paying the ransom. The bandits came to the village to urge the ransom and burned two piles of rapeseed. Yesterday (July 31), the second team of the county water patrol team reported that a bandit boat was docked at Xiaomiaogang outside the West Gate. The team dispatched to encircle and suppress the bandits, shot down a bandit boat and rescued the kidnapped victim, Lin Xiangyun. He is now being escorted to the team headquarters to wait for his family to pick him up.

Wuxi

Young Man Impersonating a Military Officer Arrested

The county government of this county secretly ordered martial law on the previous day (July 31) for a certain anniversary. Officers and police from the Public Security Bureau's detective team patrolled the roads, docks, and train stations day and night. At about 1:00 am, detective Wang Shuanglin saw six young men, one of whom was wearing a military uniform, entering and leaving the First Hotel, Datong Hotel, and Railway Hotel on the road. Detective Wang saw that their behavior was suspicious and immediately telegraphed the Second Branch of the Public Security Bureau, requesting that Bureau Chief Liu Qingtai and patrol leaders Gu and Zhang lead the police to the First and Datong Hotels and arrest Xu Yuncheng, Gu Shouwei, and four others. Military uniforms, a symbol of Chen of the 19th Route Army Student Volunteer Army, and many letters were found. They were taken to the bureau together. After a preliminary trial by Bureau Chief Zhu, the case was deemed to involve impersonating a military officer and was submitted to the County Public Security Bureau for review yesterday.

Changshu Chamber of Commerce Meeting on Business Tax

The Jiangsu Province rectification of business tax case has been decided by the provincial government meeting. According to the tax rate approved by the Ministry of Finance, and with reference to the compromise measures of Zhejiang Province, it is set as a three-level system, namely 5/1000, 8/1000, and 10/1000, a total of three types. However, the rice and noodle industry, although listed as 5/1000, will temporarily be taxed at 2/1000. Regulations have been drafted and special bureaus will be established, which will be implemented in the autumn of this year. The provincial government has requested the Chamber of Commerce to follow the resolution of the previous meeting and the intention of official-merchant cooperation, and to transfer to the various chambers of commerce for joint assistance. The Chamber of Commerce has approved the letter and has separately written to the chambers of commerce in each district to convene meetings separately and report the results as soon as possible so that they can be submitted to the Executive Committee Standing Committee on the 11th of this month for joint discussion in order to achieve unity. All five county chambers of commerce in the former Changzhou Prefecture, namely Wujin, Wuxi, Yixing, Jiangyin, and Jingjiang, are scheduled to meet on the 8th, convened and managed by the Wujin County Chamber of Commerce.

Change of Education Bureau Director

Lu Renshou, Director of the Wuxi County Education Bureau, has repeatedly submitted his resignation, which has been reviewed and approved by Zhou Fohai, Director of the Department of Education, and Jiangdu native Gu You has been appointed as his successor. Director Gu has come to Wuxi the day before yesterday and took office at the bureau yesterday morning. He has drafted definite measures for the education funds in Wuxi, as well as the issuance of outstanding education fees, and has adopted a tight fiscal policy for internal staff and education administrative expenses in order to save expenses.

Farmers in Yangyuanli Encounter Thieves in the Black Night

Jiang Helin, a farmer in Yangyuanli near Huangtutang in the seventh district (Huai Shang) of the county, is a well-to-do family. Recently, his wife received a cooperative fund of more than 70 yuan, which was coveted by thieves. The day before yesterday in the middle of the night, eight bandits with bayonets broke into the house and searched everywhere. It is estimated that they were robbed of more than 70 yuan in cash and gold ornaments, totaling a loss of about 300 yuan. Afterwards, because the bandits were all local poor people, they were afraid of retaliation and did not dare to report to the county.

Changzhou

Anti-Japanese Association Seizes a Large Quantity of Hate Goods

The Wuyi Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association has recently received secret reports from Shanghai stating that a large quantity of hate goods was being transported to the area. The association's director, Yang Yin, along with inspectors, immediately launched a thorough investigation. On the afternoon of the 31st, at around 5:00 PM, they discovered a cargo ship near Huimin Bridge. While inspecting the ship, Zhang Wenming, a clerk from the Qianqiufang Hengshun Foreign Goods Store, invited Yang and others to the store to talk, attempting to bribe them to release the cargo ship. Yang and others explained the importance of righteousness and immediately reported to the Anti-Japanese Association and the County Party Headquarters, transporting all the goods to the shore. Those without suspicion were immediately returned to their respective owners. A total of 14 items were sent to the Anti-Japanese Association, transported by Hengshuntai, Taichang, Shengtixiang, Qingchangyu, and other firms.

Business Tax Assessment Increased

The original business tax assessment for Wuyi County last year was 140,000 yuan, but the County Chamber of Commerce only managed to collect 56,000 yuan. Due to the impact of the Shanghai war, even the assessed amount could not be fully collected. This year, in the spring and summer seasons, the Finance Department sent personnel to collect the tax. The investigation procedures have not yet been completed. Recently, the Finance Department appointed Lu Fengtai as the director, and the assessment has been increased to between 180,000 and 270,000 yuan, scheduled to take effect from the autumn season.

Nantong

Defense Funding Reduction Issue

The total defense expenditure for Nantong County was originally set at 240,000 yuan annually. The provincial government now considers this excessive and has reduced it by half. Currently, various district militias have had to dismiss their recruits and switch to conscripting volunteer militia due to the budget cuts.

Jiangyin

Suspicious Death of Sister, Brother Seeks Justice

In Miaobangdou area near Yuanjiawei in the southern countryside of this city, there is a wealthy villager named Yuan Shishan, who has always been on bad terms with his wife, Zhu. They often argued and even physically assaulted each other. On the night of July 20th, the couple argued again over trivial matters. The next morning, Zhu was found to have hanged herself, with injuries all over her body and bloodstains around her mouth and nose. The sight of her death was extremely tragic. Upon seeing the body, her mother was overwhelmed with grief and confronted Yuan about it. Yuan then asked a village head to intercede on his behalf, agreeing to provide ample clothing, a coffin, and conduct funeral rites and prayers to quell the matter. However, Zhu Xincheng, the deceased's brother, felt that his sister's death was unclear. He reported the matter to the Hefu Public Security Substation the day before yesterday. It is reported that the substation has forwarded the case to the Wuxing District Court for investigation.

Gaoyou

Suspects Arrested in Major Robbery Case

On the evening of the 27th of this month, at 9:00 PM, the home of Song Shuchi, the former director of the telegraph office, located in Houguanyin, south of this city's south gate, was robbed by six bandits. Silver dollars, clothing, and other items were stolen, resulting in a significant loss. The case has been reported to the county government, which has ordered a strict investigation. This city's First Public Security Bureau received a secret report this morning (the 30th) stating that a traveler named Jiang Zhenpeng, residing in the Houguanyin Nanyuan Hotel for several days, was highly suspected in the Song case. The bureau's inspector, Cai Chengnan, led police officers to the hotel. At that time, Jiang Zhenpeng was playing mahjong at the home of Li Song. Inspector Cai then led the police to Li's house, arrested Jiang, and brought him and three other gamblers back to the bureau. During the preliminary hearing, Jiang claimed to be a special agent of the 24th squad of the 6th District Water Police and denied involvement in the robbery. The bureau is now preparing a document to send the suspect and others to the county government for interrogation.

Jiaxing

Kidnapping Incident Occurs in Xushan Township

In the Shanbang area of Xushan Township, Hantang District, Jiaxing, two bandit ships suddenly arrived at midnight on the 30th. More than 30 bandits, speaking in a mixture of Wenzhou and Taizhou dialects, forced their way into the home of Wu Changfu, a farmer in the area, with torches and weapons. They severely beat Changfu and his wife and four others, causing serious injuries. They then proceeded to loot the house, also targeting the home of Wu Danchi, who lived in the same residence. Before leaving, they kidnapped Changfu's eight-year-old son, named Jinguan, and took him aboard the ship, then roared away. The victims reported the incident to the local public security authorities that night, who ordered the police to pursue the bandits, but their whereabouts are currently unknown.

Huzhou

Barber Assassinated in Xiagang

Wang Linpei, a barber in Xiagang Town, west of the city, was over forty years old and married to a woman named Gu. Yesterday (the 30th), at around 10:00 PM, Linpei was already asleep, while Gu was still outside the door cooling off. Suddenly, she heard her husband cry out in pain from inside the room. She rushed inside and saw that he had been stabbed in the lower abdomen, and the bed was covered in blood. He was barely alive, and the assailant had already fled without a trace. The reason for the assassination may be related to jealousy. Today (the 31st), the injured man's condition has not worsened, and his life is not in danger.

Sixth District Militia Captures Kidnappers

The Sixth District Militia and the Huangtu First Independent Brigade captured a kidnapper named Liu Heshang and his hostage, Xie Yuankang, a 16-year-old middle school student from Xiejiatoucun, Maojiaqiao, outside Changzhou, behind Qiuzhuang Qinglong Mountain. They were escorted to Huangtu. Liu Heshang escaped, and the suspects Zhang Yungeng, Gao Zhengui, Yü Quanfu, the boatman, and Gu Xiaopei, who allowed Liu the bandit to escape, along with the hostage Xie Yuankang, were all escorted to the county government for interrogation and detention yesterday morning (the 31st) at around 1:00 AM.

Hangzhou

Seventeen-Year-Old Maid Raped

Su Zhen, the 17-year-old daughter of Shen Mo, a village woman from Wanjia Pavilion in Banshan, Hang County, was introduced by a neighbor to work as a maid at the Wang Fulian (also known as Yongzhao) clothing store near the Bodhi Jing She in West Lake due to poverty and difficulty in obtaining food and clothing. It was agreed that her monthly salary would be two yuan. The girl slept in a shed behind the house at night. Unexpectedly, Wang found the girl to be quite attractive and, being from the same village, became lustful. One night, he sneaked into the shed while she was asleep and raped her using violent means. The next day, he gave her a silk dress and a bracelet, enticing her to become his concubine. The girl realized she had been deceived and fled to the Cui and Li families. Wang came and created a commotion, and the police were called to escort him to the court. After investigation by prosecutor Zhou, it was determined that there was reasonable suspicion of rape, and Wang Yongzhao and Wang Zhang were ordered to be detained pending investigation. The girl Su Zhen was taken back by her mother to await further proceedings.

German Secretly Exploits Mineral Resources in Zhejiang Province

The provinces of Zhejiang are rich in mineral deposits. The Mineral Resources Survey Institute of the Construction Department sent personnel to various counties to investigate and discovered many new mining areas. However, due to a lack of capital for exploitation, they have attracted the attention of foreigners who are secretly exploiting them. It has come to the Construction Department's attention that, according to a telegram from the Liancheng Mineral Company, a German named Pu Dixi is secretly exploiting the Shipingzhou mine in Qingtian County. They have requested that the county be ordered to investigate and handle the matter according to the law. Yesterday, a telegram reported that the first batch of 20 tons of secretly mined ore sand has been transported from Ruoxi to the Wenzhou customs office, ready for shipment to Shanghai. Upon receiving the telegram, the Construction Department immediately telegraphed the county magistrate, ordering him to investigate and report the matter as soon as possible.

Sports

1932 Davis Cup Concludes

American Vines Defeats Cochet 3-2 Total Result: France Reclaims Victory with 3-2

In the 1932 Davis Cup, France ultimately defeated the United States 3-2, retaining the championship for the sixth year. The results of the final three singles and doubles matches between the French and American players have been reported previously. In the final singles match, Vines defeated Cochet 3-2, with scores of 4-6, 0-6, 7-5, 8-6, and 6-2, leading to a final score of 3-2, with France claiming victory.

List of Davis Cup Champions

The Davis Cup world tennis tournament began in 1900 and has been held for 32 years. The European War interrupted the tournament for four years. A list of the past champions is as follows:

1900-1902 (3 times) United States

1903-1906 (4 times) Great Britain

1907-1911 (5 times) Australia

1912 (1 time) Great Britain

1913 (1 time) United States

1914 (1 time) Australia

1915-1918 European War - Tournament Suspended

1919 (1 time) Australia

1920-1926 (7 times) United States

1927-1932 (6 times) France

Total: 29 Competitions

United States: 11 times

Australia: 7 times

France: 6 times

Great Britain: 5 times

French Domination Stuns the World

Looking at the past 29 competitions, the United States and Great Britain initially shared dominance. Then Australia rose to prominence and held the lead for five years. After the European War, the situation changed. After winning once in Australia, the United States won the championship for seven consecutive years, proudly declaring itself the world leader. Then France rose to prominence, with its "Four Musketeers" achieving great success and defeating all opponents to seize the Davis Cup. For the past six years, they have consistently defended their title and are showing a tendency to gradually surpass the United States in the number of victories.

Borotra's Hard Work and Great Contributions

Speaking of this year's competition, France's retention of the championship is largely due to Borotra. In the two singles matches, he defeated his opponents entirely through his superior technique. In the third-day singles match, he particularly demonstrated his ability to survive in a desperate situation. A single mistake could have led to a huge error. The key to his success was his maturity, stability, and skillful use of his strengths. One person's efforts have brought honor to an entire nation. Borotra's hard work and contributions are truly commendable.

The United States' Failure Is Blamed on Vines

The world regarded Vines, the young American player considered the second Tilden, as disappointing in this final. Before the competition, people generally believed that the United States had a better chance of winning. The United States' doubles team was almost certain to win. The key to victory lay in the four singles matches. With Vines on the team, the United States could have been carefree. However, the young general's skills were good, but his experience was lacking. In the first match, he made mistakes due to nervousness and was defeated by Borotra. Although the entire team later put in extra effort, it was difficult to reverse the situation. They watched as the French players seized the Davis Cup.

10th World Games, Day 2: Liu Changchun Fails to Qualify in 100m Heat

Fifth in Second Heat of Preliminaries | To Participate in 200m Heat Today New World Record in Women's Javelin | US Leads Athletics with 27 Points

Over 100,000 Spectators

| Mild Weather, High Spirits |

(Special Dispatch from Dentsu, Los Angeles, 31st) The athletics competition, the main attraction of the Games, began at 2:00 PM today at the Olympic Stadium. The grandstands, with a capacity of over 100,000 people, were filled with men and women. Southern California's summer climate, with its lush green grass, perfectly complemented the green fields of the athletic ground. The weather was mild and suitable for sports. The nervous athletes from various countries stood in the corridors of the rest area, waiting for their turn. Cheerleaders and strategists also boosted morale and encouraged the athletes, hoping for victory. The Games commenced amidst tension, excitement, and complete silence.

(Special Telegram from Los Angeles, 31st) Today is the second day of the Games. The weather is excellent. As it is Sunday, the stands are packed with spectators, leaving almost no room to stand. The track and field events started at 2:00 PM, beginning with the 400m hurdles preliminaries.

Finishes Fifth in Second Heat | To Participate in 200m Heat Today

Our Chinese athlete Liu Changchun participated in the first preliminary heat of the 100m on the 31st. Despite his efforts in the second heat, he finished fifth and failed to qualify. Mr. Liu will participate in the first preliminary heat of the 200m today (2nd).

New Records Set at the Games

American Woman Sets New World Record in Javelin

Eddie Tolan's 100m Time is 10.4 Seconds

Shot Put and 10,000m are Also New Game Records

The athletics competition began on the second day of the Games. In the second preliminary heat of the 100m, Eddie Tolan (USA) ran 10.4 seconds, Metcalfe (USA) 10.7 seconds, and Wykoff 10.5 seconds, all setting new Games records (the original record was 10.8 seconds). It is expected that the final race, in addition to the aforementioned three, will also feature intense competition from Simpson (USA) and Yoshioka (Japan). In the 10,000m final, the Finnish athletes were surprisingly defeated by the Polish athlete Kusociński. Kusociński's time of 30 minutes 11.4 seconds was a new Games record, breaking the previous record of 30 minutes 18.8 seconds held by Nurmi of Finland, but it still did not surpass Nurmi's world record of 30 minutes 6.2 seconds. In the women's javelin final, Ms. Didrikson of the United States set a new world record with a throw of 43.68 meters, breaking the previous world record of 42.32 meters held by Ms. Schluma of Germany. Sexton's shot put of 52 feet 6 inches (16.01 meters) was also a new Games record. American track and field athlete Sexton won the shot put championship.

The Progress of the 10,000 Meter Final

(Special Dispatch from Dentsu, Los Angeles, 21st) The 100m final, a highlight of the first day, started at 5:00 PM. The strong runners from Northern Europe, Iso-Hollo and the rising giant from Poland, Kusociński, ran at breakneck speed from start to finish. Later, Kusociński, Iso-Hollo, and Virtanen broke away as a group. Their lightning speed was a sight to behold. Until the final sprint, they were neck and neck, making for a fierce race. The Japanese athlete Kitamoto was in 8th place until the first lap, while Takenaka was in 11th. Although they tried their best to catch up, Kitamoto fell to 11th by the 8th lap, and Takenaka fell to 13th. By the 14th lap, Takenaka was a lap behind Kusociński. In the last 20 laps, Kusociński and Iso-Hollo ran even harder. After a great battle between the two, Kusociński finally surpassed Iso-Hollo with 200 meters to go, taking first place. Kitamoto was 800 meters behind Kusociński, in 12th place, and Takenaka was in 13th.

Record of the First Day of the Chemistry Discussion

Divided into Three Groups for Discussion

Nanjing, 1st - The Education Chemistry Discussion held a general meeting on the 1st. Chen Kezhong, Chairman of the Ministry of Education, reported on the motives for convening the discussion and the preparations made, and explained the scope and objectives to be achieved by the group discussions. A total of 40 members attended, and three groups were immediately formed to address national defense chemistry courses, taxation standards, and chemistry translation names. Each member identified one or two groups. In the afternoon, the presidium was elected, and in addition to Chairman Chen from the Ministry of Education, Chen Yuguang and Zeng Zhaolun were elected as the presidium for the Translation and Curriculum Standards Group, and Wang Xinyan, Wang Jiliang, and Cheng Yingzhang were elected as the presidium for the National Defense Chemistry Group.

Jinan University Students Petition the Overseas Chinese Affairs Commission

The Student Union, Overseas Chinese Student Union, and Shanghai Alumni Association of the National Jinan University in Shanghai, are organizing a school protection movement due to the Ministry of Education's decision to merge the university's Law and Education departments. Representatives Wei Zhenhua, Xie Shaobai, Hu Shouyu, and others went to Beijing to petition various parties. Yesterday, Wei Zhenhua, Lin Ping, and others went to the Overseas Chinese Affairs Commission to appeal for assistance. Chairman Chen Shuren, Vice-Chairman Zhou Qigang, Standing Committee Member Huang Jichen, Education Director Chen Kewen, and Committee Member Xu Tongxiong, among others, received them and expressed their willingness to stand on the side of the interests of overseas Chinese and provide strong assistance. During the meeting, Wei Zhenhua and others were invited to attend and report on the reasons for opposing the merger. It is rumored that a resolution will be passed to request the Executive Yuan to revoke the established decision.

The Labor University Student School Protection Group issued a letter to students nationwide yesterday, requesting assistance. Xue Long, Gao Zongyi, attended the meeting of university student representatives convened by Jinan University students the day before and was elected as a committee member.

First Day of the Meeting on Curriculum Standards for Primary and Secondary Schools

Revisions to the Curriculum System for Secondary School Subjects; No Major Changes to the Provisional Curriculum Standards for Primary Schools

Nanjing, 1st - The Curriculum Standards Revision Committee for Primary and Secondary Schools held a meeting at the Ministry of Education starting at 9:00 AM on the 1st. Over 40 primary and secondary education experts attended. Chairman Gu Shusen reported on the Ministry of Education's opinions on the revision of the primary and secondary school curriculum, and discussed common revisions to the primary and secondary school curriculum. In the afternoon, primary and secondary school groups held separate meetings. The primary school group resolved: (1) to revise the general outline of the curriculum item by item, (2) to make no major changes to the provisional curriculum standards, with only slight revisions to the content, wording, and style, (3) to publish the moral education standards at the same time as the curriculum standards, and (4) to designate subject-specific committees to refer to the common revision points and revise them separately. The secondary school group resolved to heavily revise the curriculum system for secondary school subjects and passed revisions to the curriculum timetable for junior high schools. The meeting adjourned at 6:00 PM. Later, Zhu Jiahua hosted a banquet for all committee members at the White Palace Hotel. The meeting will continue on the 2nd.

Another telegram: According to the discussion results, the secondary school curriculum will emphasize natural sciences and change the grading system to focus on teaching time. There will be fewer revisions to the primary school curriculum, which will be submitted to experts for review and then brought to the meeting for discussion.

Free Talk

Quotations from the 93-Year-Old Ma Xiangbo

Where is Vladivostok?

— Written by Han

Chinese people's lives are worthless, their reputation is worthless, and their territory is even more worthless. In the last hundred years, I don't know how much of our beautiful land has been lost in confusion! I read foreign books as early as the sixth year of Xianfeng, so I knew something about geography. At that time, I already knew that the area north of the Heilongjiang River was ours, and Sakhalin Island was also ours. I also knew that Sakhalin Island had a special product called seahorse, and the skin of the seahorse was very valuable. At that time, Sakhalin Island paid tribute to China every year, and seahorse was a special feature of the tribute. The customs of Sakhalin Island were also very different from those of China. For example, in Sakhalin Island, deer were used as cattle for farming and pulling carts, which was not seen in mainland China.

Now that the situation in Rehe is urgent, I am reminded of Rehe. Rehe was a summer resort for the emperors of the Qing Dynasty. Rehe had a hunting ground as large as a prefecture, specially for the emperor to gallop and hunt. In the tenth year of Xianfeng, the Anglo-French Allied Forces captured Beijing. In August of that year, Emperor Xianfeng fled to Rehe, and Prince Gong temporarily took charge. At that time, many eunuchs and palace maids followed, and even the grass paper used by the palace maids had to be paid for by the national treasury. This is a very ugly historical fact!

When Vladivostok was taken by the Russians, the imperial court didn't even know where Vladivostok was. The Prime Minister's Office telegraphed the governors of various provinces, but no one could respond. At that time, I happened to be the director of the Shandong Qikou Machinery Bureau. The governor of Shandong asked me, and I pointed out the location of Vladivostok to them. At that time, it was impossible to find a map. Later, it was finally found in a church in the Shandong countryside. Think about it, such a big China didn't even have a map, the boundaries were not clear, and the latitude and longitude lines were not recognized. With such confusion, the territory would inevitably be lost sooner or later.

Speaking of borders and maps, there are two very valuable historical materials.

Zheng Hongnian on the Difficulty of Finding a Job

— Shi Yan Ye

The number of unemployed people in China today is the highest record in the history of unemployment statistics in the world. As far as the knowledge class is concerned, not only those with meager skills cannot find a place to eat, but even students, even those who have returned from studying in the East and West, are often unemployed. As the school year comes to an end, millions of graduates leave school, and the society has millions more unemployed people. The graduates of National Jinan University are very numerous this year. The students believe that their president, Zheng Hongnian, has a reputation and knows many dignitaries. They asked him to find them jobs. Zheng said to them with emotion: "The officialdom of today is not suitable to enter, nor can it be entered. Those who become officials all come to eat. Since they become officials to eat, they naturally regard public affairs as light and how to enrich their personal lives as important. And it's not just for the life of one person. Their relatives and friends who cannot live are also attached to them and help them solve the problem of eating. The rice in the officialdom has been eaten by them, so why should we want to share a cup of soup with them? My youngest son has just returned from the New World. What he studied was diplomacy. He planned to obtain a superior position in the diplomatic world to display his talents. He asked me to find a way. So I wrote to Foreign Minister Luo. I was fortunate enough to receive a reply, but only a vacant position as a consultant to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs. With my knowledge and my son's qualifications as a student abroad, that's all I got. What can you university students expect? But please don't be discouraged. I will do my best to help you." This is what the graduates of Jinan University told me. It is very difficult to find a job.

The Terror of Tiger Might

— Gu Dai

The heat this summer reached its highest degree, setting a new record at the observatory, and the duration of the heat was unprecedented in the past eight years, resulting in a severe epidemic in the Songhu area, which was rare in recent years. The situation is so miserable that it cannot be overstated. I dare to write down what I have seen and heard and publish it in this talk. I deeply hope that those who read my article will persuade their relatives, friends, and neighbors to get vaccinated as soon as possible for prevention. Its merit should far outweigh the support of charitable undertakings.

One of my relatives lives near the Guandi Temple in Ximen. The wife, a certain female, has never liked Western medicine. After the Shanghai war this year, the epidemic was bound to be severe. The newspaper has repeatedly reported it. Her husband persuaded her to go to the health bureau to get vaccinated. The woman said, "I have never been vaccinated in my life. I am already twenty-five years old. Why bother?" A week later, she went to her relative's house for a party. When she returned, she vomited and diarrhea. Her husband was afraid and planned to send her to the hospital, but the woman refused. He planned to hire a doctor for treatment, but the woman refused again. After a delay of half a day, the illness worsened. Her mind gradually failed. Her husband saw that the situation was not good and urgently hired a doctor for treatment, but the doctor could do nothing.

There is a woman surnamed Mou on Xilin Road in Ximen. She is usually strong and manages the housework in an orderly manner. One day, at lunch, she suddenly thought of eating soy sauce pork. She bought it and ate it with her husband. After the meal, she was very thirsty and bought a bottle of soda water and drank it. By evening, she felt slightly unwell. In an instant, her complexion changed drastically, as white as ashes. Her teeth were clenched tightly. Her husband was panicked when he saw this and tried to pry open her teeth with his fingers to feed her with ten drops of water, but her teeth would not move. In a hurry, he used a copper spoon from the table to pry it open. Unexpectedly, the spoon was bitten off by the woman and swallowed into her stomach. In less than a quarter of an hour, she suddenly died. More than three hours later, her chest and abdomen were still warm. She left behind a daughter, who was only three months old. It was extremely tragic.

In a certain village in Jiangwan Township, there was an old man named Hu Er who lived in a hut with his old wife, daughter-in-law, and two grandchildren. After the war, life was already extremely difficult. Unexpectedly, Hu Er's son suddenly died of tiger plague. He was hastily buried. The next morning, Hu Er's second grandson also died of the epidemic. By evening, Hu Er also vomited and diarrhea. He died at dawn. At midnight, Hu Er's eldest grandson also died. Of the six people in the family, four died within three days. Only two generations of widows were left. Although these two generations of widows did not die in the Japanese army's artillery fire and were lucky enough to escape from the tiger's mouth, their future is difficult, and their food and clothing cannot be sustained. It is also very pitiful. This is what I heard on a trip to Jiangwan yesterday. The narrator is a neighbor of Hu Er, so what he said should not be false.

Different Past and Present

— Jin Junren

A friend told me that there is a saying in the essays of Life Weekly, "wind, horse, and ox principle." He asked me to guess its meaning. I said, "It's nothing more than 'as incompatible as wind, horses, and oxen'." The friend said, "No, no. In the past, people said that wind, horses, and oxen were incompatible. Now, wind, horses, and oxen cannot be separated for a moment." The friend knew that I had not read the newspaper, so he told me the general idea below.

"Wind" means to show off. "Horse" means to flatter. "Ox" means to boast. It means that today's people can do nothing but show off, flatter, and boast. Conversely, if one is good at showing off, flattering, and boasting, then the skills of getting along in the world are all encompassed, and there is no need to seek more abilities.

After listening to my friend, I couldn't help but laugh and admire the author's ingenuity in picking up the wisdom of the ancients and making his own wonderful article. Waste utilization could not be more profitable than this.

Think about it, today's people go out in cars and horses, live in foreign buildings, and have concubines flattering them and servants serving them. As for clothing, they wear summer clothes in summer and fur clothes in winter. As for food, they eat all kinds of delicacies. The pleasure of the body is truly beyond imagination. Those who see it praise it and envy it endlessly. It can be said that they are showing off to the fullest. But when you investigate the origin of their showing off, what is not the result of flattering and boasting? The past and present are different. There are many differences. I never thought that the immortal text would also change with the times. Isn't it strange?

Medical News: Medical Doctor Liu Junshi Hong graduated from Nanyang Medical University. He then went to various famous hospitals in Germany and Japan for many years of internship. He has a good understanding of internal medicine, especially diseases of the lungs, intestines, stomach, and nerves. After returning to China, he served as the director of internal medicine in major hospitals in China. Whenever there are difficult and complicated diseases, they are cured immediately after Dr. Liu's diagnosis and treatment. For example, my wife had suffered from lung disease for a long time and had been examined by Chinese and Western doctors, but it recurred from time to time because the root cause was not removed. Since last year, after Dr. Liu's acupuncture and medicine, the disease was cured and the root was removed in less than a month, and it has not recurred since then. My eldest and second daughters suffered from weak bodies and brain damage due to excessive study, and their nerves were stimulated, so they were plagued by illness for a long time and were treated repeatedly without recovery. Now they have also been cured by Dr. Liu's diagnosis. From this, I believe that Dr. Liu's academic knowledge and experience are indeed very rich and far from being comparable to those who only pursue false reputations. (Dr. Liu's Clinic) is now located at No. 21 Pobo Lane, Luban Road, French Concession (Xu Langxi)

Imagist Paintings on the Yangtze River (Part 2)

— Shazhou

(5) Unreasonable Stop

Abroad, it is already shameful for us to be discriminated against and bullied by foreigners, but thinking a step back, that is after all a foreign country, and we can still be less angry. But to be discriminated against by foreigners in our own country is unbearable.

When our ship arrived in Jiujiang, a piece of news spread like a storm throughout the entire cabin, adding a layer of anxiety to the hearts of many passengers who were in charge of duties. And this news finally became a concrete fact: it was decided that the ship would stop in Jiujiang for one night. The reason for stopping the ship was ridiculous. It was said that four Westerners on board were going to Guling to escape the summer heat. To get to Guling, they would of course have to disembark in Jiujiang. But even when they arrived in Jiujiang, they still refused to go ashore. Why? They said it was late and they didn't want to stay in Chinese-run hotels, so they had to stay on the ship for another night, and the precious time of more than five hundred Chinese passengers was sacrificed for the sake of those four people.

The next morning, it was already eight o'clock, but the ship still showed no sign of moving. What was the reason for this again? It was said that the four people going to Guling were having breakfast. After a while, it still didn't move, because one of the four was in the WC.

The entire ship of passengers was furious.

"Foreign devils are sent to Jiangxi."

"We Chinese are really hopeless."

Such angry curses could be heard everywhere, but they were too weak and useless in practice! But what reason do I have to say that they are weak? Forget it, if you don't improve yourself, then there is nothing unbearable about being bullied by foreigners.

(6) Fragmentary Notes

There are no Chinese passengers on the Nissin Shipping Company's ships. This shows China's anger towards the Japanese, but we must use the same spirit to deal with the ships of any country. Otherwise, the money will still flow to other countries if it doesn't flow to Japan!

Among the mountains on both sides of the Yangtze River, Mount Lu is the highest.

Huangshi Port is in eastern Hubei, and the scenery is excellent. The area produces iron, which is mined by the Japanese. China does not take its own wealth, which is the biggest reason for China's poverty.

The Yangtze River is China's main artery, but what can we see on this artery? Apart from the vast river water and the towering mountains, there are only warships flying foreign flags. If China is a sleeping lion, then will it really "sleep soundly for five thousand years"? (Quote from Wang Jingwei's poem "Ancient Cypress in Jinci")

Striking the Bell in the Ancient Temple (62)

— Bu Chu Ting Cao Zhai Fu

Sixty-Nine

This ancient temple labor-study group occupies all my thoughts. When I was taking a walk in the courtyard after dinner, the ancient temple labor-study group floated up from my mind again. In a flash, many questions came one after another asking me to answer them. [What's the point of rigidly treating a factory as a factory? What's the point of rigidly treating a school as a school? What's the point of rigidly treating a society as a society?] Everyone is probably afraid that I will be arbitrary, right? My answer is... [There's no point in rigidly running a factory, rigidly running a school, or rigidly doing social work! Because doing it this way is tearing apart life and disintegrating living cells. Therefore, everyone who runs it is overwhelmed and cannot find a way out. What is the meaning of the life of an executioner! If you run a factory, if you also pay attention to the opportunities for the workers to grow and the relationship of equality and mutual assistance, it will immediately become a meaningful factory. If you run a school, if you also pay attention to the opportunities for teachers and students to produce and the relationship of equality and mutual assistance, it will immediately become a meaningful school. If you are transforming a society, if you also pay attention to the opportunities for production and growth of each member, it will immediately become a meaningful society.] I finally seemed to be even more enlightened. The change of name is only a formality. If running a business contains these three meanings, then it can be called a school, a factory, or a society. If these three meanings are not integrated, even if it is labeled as a labor-study group, it is no different from hanging a sheep's head and selling dog meat. When I thought of being excited, I told Mr. Zhu everything. He said... [Your reasoning is indeed correct. The meaning of the labor-study group is not the name of the labor-study group, which will turn all longer-lasting life groups into meaningful groups. In ancient times, the family was almost a small labor-study group. Several famous Chinese armies are large-scale labor-study groups. Any group that is more permanent, if it does not contain the meaning of the labor-study group, will become a boring life and lead to aging. No group can be run rigidly. For example, prisons, if they are run rigidly, are worse than hell. Think about it, if all the prisons in the country were turned into labor-study groups, what a meaningful thing that would be! Think again, if all the families, shops, factories, schools, armies, and villages in the country were turned into labor-study groups! Everyone produces, everyone grows, everyone is equal and helps each other, everyone defends themselves and defends others! Then what a solemn country the Republic of China would become! The new life of the Chinese nation is latent in the seeds of the labor-study group. Gardeners, spread them widely!]

Foreign Exchange Rate Slightly Lower, Interbank Loan Rate Firm and High

Although many Chinese banks were open for business, it was difficult to investigate because the acceptance of collection procedures was not as convenient as usual. New York Stock Market Weekly Review

(Report from American Eastern Banking Corporation)

Since the middle of this month, the New York stock market has shown signs of recovery, and this week it has been improving vigorously. However, the reason for this is difficult to speculate. In short, it is nothing more than a change in investor sentiment. In the past few days, people from all over the United States have been investing in and buying stocks continuously, and the New York market has suddenly become prosperous. Low-priced stocks are especially in demand in the market. According to people in the know, if the recent buying trend can continue for some time, investor confidence will become more solid, and the stock market will not see a reversal again. It is estimated that in one week, industrial stocks rose by 6.05, railway stocks rose by 4.17, and public utility stocks rose by 3.80. The rise in government bonds was even more rapid than that of stocks. Yarn Exchange Increases Two-Account Commission

The Yarn Exchange Brokers Association received a letter from the Exchange's Board of Directors stating that a meeting of all brokers would be held at 3:00 PM in the Exchange's second market to discuss all proposals regarding the increase in the two-account commission for cotton yarn. (1) The original cotton commission for two accounts was 2.5 taels per 100 piculs, now increased by 1 tael to 3.5 taels. (2) The original cotton yarn commission for two accounts was 10 taels per 100 pieces, now increased by 2.5 taels to 12.5 taels. However, this issue was not unanimously passed and will be discussed at the next meeting. There is no change to other commissions.

Zhejiang Construction Department Sells Autumn Silkworm Seeds

The seed price is determined by the department and paid after the sale of cocoons. Disinfection, warming, and stability are guided by the household, and no additional fees are charged.

Zhejiang Construction Minister Zeng Jian, in view of the fact that the farmers in the silkworm areas under his jurisdiction suffered great losses from the spring and summer silkworms raised this year due to weather damage, and the agricultural silkworm economy was on the verge of bankruptcy, has now decided to rescue the autumn silkworms, select and purchase high-quality autumn silkworm seeds, and distribute them to households according to the number of households. The seed price is determined by the department and paid after the sale of cocoons. All matters such as disinfection, warming and shared raising, and sending personnel to guide households are the responsibility of the department, and no additional fees are charged, in order to help agricultural silkworms.

Zhenmei Green Tea Selling Well in Europe

Only Gongxi Tea is Being Watched by Russian Merchants

Yushan Tea Firm Has Not Yet Closed

In previous years, the low-grade tea from Yushan and other roads in Jiangxi Province was sold very sluggishly by foreign merchants. This year, various firms have turned their attention to low-grade and cheap green tea because the high-grade goods from Wutun in Anhui Province are too expensive and unprofitable to transport and sell. Recently, sales have been particularly smooth. Therefore, Yushan Tea Firm plans to add new tea and Zizhuang after selling the first two batches. The production of tea trees in Qianyushan and Yushan differs from that of Anhui. The tea leaves develop in spring, summer, and autumn. In short, as long as the firm needs it, the mountain households can collect and supply it endlessly. At the moment, tea firms with more abundant capital and more stable sales are still waiting to close the market and still have the potential to add tea and continue to make it.

Wuyuan Stored Tea Has Been Sold Out

The new tea from various villages in Beiyuan here was delayed due to late harvesting and production, and the market in Shanghai tended to fall. The tea firms here all suppressed prices and bought stingily. The mountain households initially did not expect the market to be sluggish for a long time, and most were unwilling to sell cheaply, so they stored more than 2,000 dan, and no one inquired about it. Until the Shanghai market turned around at the beginning of this month, the mountain households were forced to sell early due to the poverty of the economy. The firms also reduced the cost because the mountain price was reduced, and they were happy to purchase more. In the past two weeks, the inventory in Beiyuan has been successively opened and bought up. At present, the only ones that have not been cleared are a few tea peddlers, among whom those who hoard more goods will open and make their own patterns and sell them directly in Shanghai because the purchase cost is high and they will sell them to the firms at a reduced price. At the moment, several peddlers have implemented self-made and self-sold.

Local News

Martial Law Throughout the City Yesterday

Traffic Between the French and Chinese Concessions Cut Off All Day; Some Disturbances in Various Places, Peaceful Until Late at Night

Yesterday [August 1st] was the International Labor Day (the world proletariat anti-imperialist struggle festival). The city was under special martial law. The iron gates between the Chinese and French Concessions were tightly closed. Streetcars were temporarily suspended. Only a few places had disturbances. The details are recorded as follows.

Martial Law Throughout the City

The police stations in each district of the Municipal Public Security Bureau were ordered that all police officers should be armed and on guard. Double posts were set up on all main roads. All Chinese and Western detectives of the Public Concession police were also on duty. Police cars patrolled the streets from time to time, and the joint defense was tight.

Traffic Cut Off

Starting yesterday morning, the French Concession police closed all the iron gates along the boundary between the Chinese and French Concessions, such as Xieqiao, Nanyangqiao, Xiaobeimen, Laobeimen, Xinbeimen, Xiaodongmen, etc. Only Xinkaihe was open to traffic, and Nanyangqiao Laobeimen sidewalks were open to pedestrians. A large number of Vietnamese police were sent to be armed and stationed to inspect pedestrians. The French business bus routes 5, 6, 3, and 18 were all suspended. Public Concession streetcar route 17 stopped at Dashijie, route 14 stopped at Zhengjiamuqiao, and routes 15, 16, and 19 stopped at Sanyangjingqiao. It was not restored until late at night. The Chinese business streetcar company temporarily changed route 2 from Xiaodongmen to Xuejia浜 to route 3 roundabout. The French business water and electricity company specially launched route 18 buses from Xieqiao to Dashijie.

Disturbances in Various Places

Yesterday, the Chinese Concession authorities strictly prohibited gatherings and parades. Therefore, the reactionary elements who planned to gather at the Nanshi Public Sports Ground, Huxi Caojiadu, and Zhabei Meiyuan Road were all stopped, and they were not implemented. In the morning, Zhang Mingqin, the district chief of the Sixth District Police Station, personally led the long police to patrol and seized a large number of reactionary propaganda materials on Bailinan Road and Kaixuan Road, such as [August 1 Special Issue], [August 1 Anti-Imperialist Propaganda], [Aid Niu Lan Declaration], [Workers' Daily], etc. Tao Peng Road in the Hudong District found a gathering of workers, and it was dispersed by the police. In the afternoon, workers and students who distributed leaflets were found in the Public Concession of Zhabei Meiyuan Road and Nanjing Road, and they were stopped. Only a large number of reactionary propaganda materials were seized. The security was very strict in the evening, and there was nothing wrong.

Eye Police Defense

Guowenshe said that, except for the Japanese Consulate General in Shanghai, which sent a large number of Japanese police to defend it, other consulates in Shanghai had no special traces yesterday.

Japanese Soldiers Parading

Huadong News Agency said that yesterday was the August 1 Memorial Day. At about 4 pm, more than 100 sailors from the Japanese warship Izumo, which was stationed in Shanghai, paraded in formation, going from west to east along the Bund, which was quite surprising to the general public.

Italian Minister Visited Song Yesterday

Zhang Fuyun Went to Beijing Because of Customs Affairs

Finance Minister Song Ziwen has been summoning leaders of the local banking industry and directly affiliated agencies of the Ministry of Finance for days to discuss issues such as blocking the Northeast Customs and abolishing the tael for military expenses, but there is no definite solution yet. Yesterday, those who visited Song's residence included Italian Minister Cianne and Finance Vice Minister Zou Lin. There is still no date for the implementation of the blockade. Zhang Fuyun, Director of the Customs Department, went to Beijing because of the blockade of the Northeast Customs. It is heard that the date of Song's departure from Shanghai has not been determined.

Lin Shi's Return to Beijing Postponed

Because of Important Official Business, the Trip Was Suspended

Lin Shi, Director of the Postal Department of the Ministry of Communications, has discussed the post office after the blockade of the Northeast with Director Huang Naishu after arriving in Shanghai. Lin Shi was originally scheduled to go to Beijing the night before, but the situation of the postal problem outside the customs was tense again, so he suspended his trip at the last minute and postponed his departure to Beijing. Lin went to Huang Naishu's office yesterday morning to discuss postal issues in secret for a long time. According to a reporter from Xinsheng News Agency, Lin Shi is scheduled to return to Beijing today or tomorrow.

Japan Issued 200 Passports

Huang Naishu said that the postal staff in the Liaoshen area have been repeatedly negotiated with the Japanese side by Postmaster Baridi to apply for passports, which has now been approved, but only 200 have been issued, and the pseudo-country has been ordered to issue them. There are 400 to 500 postal workers in the Northeast who urgently need to enter the customs.

Strict Arrest of Postal Workers Outside the Customs

Although the postal workers outside the customs have been ordered to stop working, the Japanese side urged the original postal staff to go to the bureau to work after forcibly taking over, otherwise they would be severely punished. The Japanese side has now issued a notice to the landlords of the postal workers to report to the police station as soon as possible so that they can be arrested.

Tianjin Sells Japanese Mail

In Tianjin, Japanese overseas Chinese have been seeking to set up a post office more urgently recently. Yesterday, according to the Xinsheng News Agency, Japanese overseas Chinese in Tianjin planned to formally set up a Japanese post office and issue Japanese stamps. The reason given by the Japanese is that this move is necessary for the convenience of communication between Japanese people. The reporter visited Song Zhumenghou, Director of the General Affairs Department of the Postal Bureau, about this matter. According to his talk, the bureau has also had an informal report on this matter. If there is such a thing, it should be consulted for the Ministry of Communications to file a protest.

Postal Workers Scattered in Jilin and Heilongjiang

The postal workers in the Jilin and Heilongjiang districts were under stricter surveillance by the Japanese. After the Administration of that place was ordered to stop, the Japanese immediately sent many policemen to Harbin, surrounded the Administration and the apartments of the staff, and forced the postal staff to work. However, the postal workers in the area were very alert and expected the Japanese to take this action, so they dispersed to other places the day before and were not arrested. Now, the Japanese have limited the postal workers in Jilin and Heilongjiang to go to the bureau to work within three days, otherwise they will be detained in accordance with the laws of the pseudo-country. As a result, all the postal workers are very frightened, change their names and hide in other places, and because they are scattered, there is no organization, so they do not know where they are and there is something to discuss.

Fifty Postal Workers Arrived in Ping

According to the Postal Administration, more than 50 postal staff in the Liaoshen District have now safely escaped and arrived in Tianjin, most of whom are lower-level personnel. Postal carriers account for more than half of them, and postal students account for only a small number. The Postal Administration plans to let these people rest for a few days. After the shock is settled, they will be given work again.

Pan Yunchao Arrives in Shanghai

Talking About the Truth of the Jehol Incident

Central Committee member Pan Yunchao, recently went from Tianjin to Beijing to discuss assisting the volunteer army with Committee member Zhu Jiqing. The discussions have been completed, and he arrived in Shanghai at 8 a.m. yesterday. He immediately went to a friend's place in the French Concession to rest, and also visited Zhu Qinglan and various organizations. After hearing the news, reporters from the New Voice Society drove to visit him, and he told them about the latest situation in the Northeast. It is recorded as follows:

The Japanese Are in a Tight Spot

Mr. Pan said, "The volunteer armies in various parts of the Northeast, due to a lack of contact and organization in the past, were unable to fight the Japanese army head-on. Therefore, they specialized in guerrilla tactics to contain their activities. Recently, as a result of efforts to engage in liaison and coordination, they have gradually become a strong group. They are only waiting for sufficient ammunition and the start of the green gauze season before they can inflict a major blow on the Japanese army. Currently, the total number of Japanese troops in the Northeast is about 150,000. Their whereabouts are still along the railway lines. The Japanese army is deeply afraid that once the railway is cut, their communication and transportation will be in danger of ending. Therefore, they spare no effort to defend it. However, their intelligence and strength are exhausted, and their embarrassing situation of being tired of running around has been completely exposed."

Attacking Chaoyang

Now, the people in the Northeast who have some assets but cannot move temporarily are still dealing with the Japanese, hoping to protect their assets and lives. Otherwise, those who can return to Guan Nei return to Guan Nei, and the rest are willing to defend their homeland and fight the Japanese to the death. As for the Jehol area, since the Japanese army bombed Chaoyang this time, the situation in Jehol is also what the people of the country urgently want to know. Before Jehol was bombed by Japanese planes, Jehol Chairman Yang Yulin still had contacts with the Japanese army on the surface because his property was still in Shenyang. A month ago, Zhang Xueliang, the director of Pingjin Pacification, sent a telegram to Yang Yulin, asking him to state his attitude so as to facilitate contact and assistance, and said that if he colluded with the Japanese, he would sever relations and not provide assistance in the future. Then Tang knew that this matter had to be explained to Zhang Xueliang to avoid misunderstanding, so he sent a representative to Beiping to meet Zhang and report the inside situation. Zhang Xueliang then understood, and the matter was heard by the Japanese, who resented Tang's failure to collude with them. Therefore, they sent a large team of planes twice to bomb Chaoyang, hoping to use intimidation to coerce Yang to obey the Japanese, but they did not succeed. At the same time, Zhang Xueliang also telegraphed Tang to take legitimate defense, and Tang also decided to resist the Japanese army. All of this is the reason before and after the Japanese army's current attempt to peep into Jehol.

Solid Defense of Pingjin

In addition, there is something to say about the terrain of Jehol and the situation of the volunteer army. In terms of terrain, Jehol is full of mountains, with undulating ridges and layers of walls. Those who have not seen the situation in Jehol, once they enter the territory, will have the suffering of winding and twisting, and it is difficult to distinguish the direction. Tang has made the most dense arrangements, and the Japanese will never be as easy to spy on as taking the three provinces of Jilin, Heilongjiang, and Shenyang. In the case of the volunteer army, the total number in Jehol is more than 200,000. They are all local people who, in view of the tragic situation of the fall of the three provinces of Jilin, Heilongjiang, and Shenyang, have risen up and joined the volunteer army. Their weapons and ammunition are well-organized due to careful preparation, and their strength is very strong. Once something happens, they can be dispatched, and they are a strong backing for the formal army. As for the defense of the Pingjin area in North China, as a result of Director Zhang's active planning, it is now extremely solid.
