New Site of Shanghai North Railway Station

The Beijing-Shanghai Passenger Transport Terminal and the Joint Transportation Station of the Two Railways are Divided into Two Places. Buying and Selling Transfers Within the Section Will be Suspended for Three Weeks Starting Yesterday. The Ministry of Railways Has Sent Xia Guangyu and Chen Yaozu to Investigate Land Prices to Prepare for Purchase. The undecided new site of the North Railway Station has been selected by the Ministry of Railways as the section south of Shida Road, north of Xiangyin Road, and along the southwest 6,000 feet of Zhongshan North Road as the site of the Beijing-Shanghai Railway Passenger Transport Terminal. The section west of Zhongshan Road, east of Zhenbei Road, and along the existing railway line, each in the north and south Thousand feet section, is the site of the Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou Railway Joint Transportation Station. The Executive Yuan, according to the Ministry of Railways, presented a decree to the municipal government the day before, and all the above-mentioned sections of the two stations were announced to suspend buying and selling transfers within three weeks from August 1, in order to facilitate surveying and purchasing. After receiving the order, the municipal government, in accordance with the provisions of Article 8, Item 1 of the Land Expropriation Law, believed that this case should be approved by the Ministry of Interior, so in addition to submitting the above situation to the Executive Yuan, it will instruct the Land Bureau today to announce in advance that within three weeks from August 1, all the above-mentioned sections of the two stations will suspend buying and selling transfers, in order to prepare for the Ministry of Railways to send personnel to survey and purchase. The Ministry of Railways has sent Counselor Xia Guangyu and Director Chen Yaozu to investigate land prices in Shanghai to prepare for purchase.

There Was a Cool Breeze and Drizzle Yesterday

There Seems to Be Typhoon Weather

Sailboats to Ningbo Suspended

Since the beginning of summer in this port, the weather has been extremely sultry, and the thermometer temperature exceeds last year's ratio. However, in recent days, a cool breeze has blown from the southeast, and the clouds in the sky are moving very fast, as if there is a typhoon. Starting yesterday, the wind was quite strong, and the weather was full of clouds, blocking the sun, and there was a drizzle. It felt quite cool to walk on the road. According to the Astronomical Observatory, the source of this cool breeze is a sign that a hurricane is about to arrive. At 4 p.m. yesterday, the Yangjingbang Observatory suspended the ball report. The strongest center point of the hurricane discovered in the Pacific Ocean two days ago has reached 26 degrees north latitude and 124 degrees east longitude and 60 miles, located directly east of Fuzhou and the northern end of Taiwan in our country. The wind is moving northwest, so it is expected that there will be storms in that area yesterday, and ships will detour. It is found that this hurricane is now tending towards the sea area of ​​Zhejiang Province in our country. If it does not change direction, it may reach Wenzhou port in the afternoon or evening today, and will reach Shanghai tomorrow. If so, the climate of this port will be cooler in a few days. According to farmers, typhoons in the middle of the heat are beneficial to the autumn harvest.

Ningbo Sailboats Do Not Sail

At noon yesterday, Taikoo and Ning Shao Shipping Companies received a report from the Astronomical Observatory, knowing that a strong wind was blowing from the southeast, had reached the sea off Wenzhou, and there was heavy rain, blowing towards the northwest, and the momentum was very rapid. Both Taikoo and Ning Shao were cautious in sailing, and temporarily announced the suspension of the New Beijing and Old Ning Shao (due to the New Ning Shao's repair and replacement) boats that should have been exported yesterday. Passengers who had boarded the ship were refunded their tickets and rescheduled to leave on Wednesday. In addition, Shanghai to Taizhou boats to Chuan Shibu and other places, Shanghai to Wenzhou ferries, etc. were also temporarily suspended from export and postponed the opening date.

Imported Sailboats Were Blocked

Commercial boats from coastal ports and the Yangtze River to Shanghai, which arrived at Wusong before 11 a.m. yesterday, all rushed into the Huangpu River and arrived in Shanghai safely. Those who arrived at Wusong after 11 o'clock, because a hurricane and rainstorm had occurred in the sea off Zhejiang and the East China Sea, chose to anchor and temporarily avoid the strong wind, and most of them were the Nanhua ferry and the boats from Japan to Shanghai. Therefore, after 11 a.m. yesterday, there were no boats entering the port, and the commercial boats that had already been exported were temporarily anchored outside Wusong.

Air Express Mail Can Be Sent Between Saigon and Marseille

Faster Than Passing Through Siberia

The Zilin Newspaper said that according to the French Oriental Airlines, all air mail sent from Saigon to Marseille and then from there to London can be reached in 14 days, which is more convenient for mail exchanges. Recently, Hong Kong tried to send 15 airmail letters, which were sent on June 7 and arrived in London on June 21, about a week faster than usual via the Siberian Railway. This test was before the Northeast Postal Incident. Today, it can be used. It was found that the mail sent from Hong Kong by the French postal ship Adou No. 2 at 4 p.m. on June 7 arrived in Saigon on June 10, and was carried by plane to Marseille the next day, arriving at 7 p.m. on June 19. It was immediately transported to Paris and handed over to Imperial Airways, and arrived in London on June 21. At present, air services between Saigon and Marseille and the proposed air postal services between Saigon and Hong Kong are two different things. The flight between Saigon and Hong Kong will be tested by the French Oriental Airlines in the near future. The planes used on the Saigon-Marseille air route also carry passengers, mail, and light goods, and fly from Saigon every Saturday morning. According to the postal authorities, all mail specially marked for acceleration will be transported by the Saigon-Marseille air route in addition to the ordinary postage and air postage.

Japanese Yarn and Cloth Transported to the Yangtze River Has Been Greatly Reduced

Traitorous Merchants Fear and Stop Operating

Just as Japanese goods were being packed, Japanese boats on the Yangtze River were also planning to openly transport Japanese goods on August 1. The situation yesterday is divided as follows:

Yarn and Cloth Transport Reduced

Japanese cotton yarn and piece goods have been transported to the Yangtze River in large quantities since June 26. At the same time, a large amount has also been exported from North China. They are all purchased by traitorous merchants and loaded by Japanese boats. Starting from August , they are planning to openly load them. Therefore, a lot of piece goods loaded from Japan to Shanghai have been recently shipped. When the Blood Soul Group warning occurred, the excited traitorous merchants mostly restrained themselves, and the large amount of piece yarn prepared to be transported to the Yangtze River on August 1 also dared not transport it. Starting yesterday, Japanese boats to the North and South Seas and the Yangtze River no longer loaded large quantities of Toyo yarn and cloth, and the export of other Japanese goods has also been greatly reduced.

Commercial Boats Refuse to Transport

Yesterday, a commercial boat in Shanghai also received a warning letter, saying that the boat was acting as a tiger's accomplice, transporting inferior goods, and buying inferior coal. A warning was given first. If it continues to load inferior goods and buy inferior coal for burning, and undertakes the sales responsibility of a certain country's goods invisibly, it will be punished and never forgiven. The boat kept this matter secret, fearing that publicity would hinder business. The letter also stated that those who privately transfer inferior goods to foreign boats for loading will also be treated as traitorous merchants. This matter has been known by some shipping industry peers. Yesterday, each boat bureau notified the crew to carefully check the goods when receiving them, so as not to transport inferior goods in a dark way, so as to avoid accidents.

County Finance Bureau Starts Collecting Land Price Tax

Abolish the Name of Silver Rice

All Combined into Foreign Codes

Shanghai County's twenty-first year of busy Tianfu has been opened by the County Finance Bureau yesterday (August 1), and starting from this session, the silver rice will be converted into foreign codes. The bureau's announcement of opening is recorded below. For announcement, according to the case, the upper and lower busy silvers in the town have been changed to concurrent collection since the eighteenth year, and the Finance Office has issued instructions to abolish the name of silver rice in the collection of busy Cao and change it to the land price tax, which will be uniformly combined into foreign codes. Starting from the twenty-first year, all reforms will be completed, etc. It is now decided to start collecting the first phase of the land price tax for the twenty-first year on August 1, limited to two months. If it exceeds two months, an additional 10% will be levied on the regular provincial and county taxes. The upper rule is that each mu of field pays 2 corners, 3 cents, 4 mils and 4 hairs of regular provincial and county tax silver, and collects 1 cent and 4 mils and 1 hair of silver for collection fee, and brings 1 corner and 6 cents of mu donation silver for education, 4 cents of donation silver for the guard group, and 4 mils of donation silver for the farm. The upper rule is that each mu of field pays a total of 4 corners, 5 cents, 2 mils and 5 hairs of silver. The quasi-rule is that each mu of field pays 2 corners, 3 cents, 7 mils and 7 hairs of regular provincial and county tax, and collects 1 cent and 4 mils and 3 hairs of silver for collection fee, 1 corner and 6 cents of mu donation silver for education, 4 cents of donation silver for the guard group, and 4 mils of donation silver for the farm. The quasi-rule is that each mu of field pays a total of 4 corners, 5 cents and 6 hairs of silver. In addition to distributing the easy-to-know single, according to Bao Tu, to various bundlers, the joint line is announced, and all the households in the town are informed, and each of them pays the required amount according to the number, and obtains a string of security, and do not wait and see and mislead yourself, so as to interfere with the questioning.

Chamber of Commerce Urges Various Industries to Prevent

Inferior Grass Felt Hats from Being Passed Off as Domestic Goods

The Chamber of Commerce, based on a letter from the grass felt hat industry in this city, stated that inferior goods have recently been found on the market that impersonate domestic products, and Hakka customers cannot distinguish them and are deceived. Yesterday, a special letter was sent to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce to forward it to various dealers to find ways to prevent it. The documents are recorded separately as follows:

Letter from the Grass Felt Hat Trade Association

Recently, it has been found that there are many inferior goods on the market that are mixed with genuine goods and borrowed the names of foreign merchants to seek meager profits. Moreover, there are even unscrupulous merchants who are so unscrupulous that they print trademarks on inferior felt hats and call them domestic products. Hakka customers cannot distinguish them and are deceived. If we do not rectify the situation urgently and find ways to prevent it, not only will the future of domestic felt hats have no foothold, but also the national economy and people's livelihood will be greatly affected. In view of this, our association has gathered 17 members of felt hat factories in the city and has taken urgent action to pursue and resist, and has established penalty rules to be jointly observed. Now, Shanghai is a central area where all merchants gather for transactions. If you are not careful, malpractices will arise, and the foreign grocery and department store industry is more likely to generate motives. For the sake of guaranteeing the future of domestic products, our association has not only published advertisements, but also applied to your association to send letters to the Department Store Industry Association, the General Merchandise Association, and related industry associations in this city, ordering them to pass on the order to their affiliated industries and pay attention to them. Please do not buy or sell inferior goods to respect the personality of the people. If any violations are found, our association will definitely announce its secret behind-the-scenes operations as much as possible, so that it will not have the support of good public opinion in the business world, and will report to the party and government organs for strict punishment. However, in the areas of various provinces, the location is remote and the road is far away, it is difficult to thoroughly understand the truth of the matter. If one leak is patched and one hundred leaks are missed, it is not a thorough solution. We also implore your association to send the printed notices to the chambers of commerce and domestic goods associations in various provinces, and ask them to forward them to their affiliated business groups for joint verification and retention. We hope that merchants in various places will know what to take and what to discard when purchasing felt hats, so that the future of domestic felt hats will be fortunate, and the domestic goods will be fortunate.

Chamber of Commerce Advises Dealers

The Chamber of Commerce sent a letter to the Foreign and Chinese General Merchandise and Department Store Associations yesterday, stating that the felt hat is popular in our country and has always relied on imports. The amount consumed by leaks has been huge throughout the years. In recent years, after the Chinese people have devoted themselves to research, all the felt hats manufactured can be compared with foreign goods, and the prices are low, which is especially popular with the Chinese people. Invisibly, foreign goods have been dealt a major blow. However, according to the letter, some profit-seeking monks dare to change the face of inferior felt hats and pass them off as domestic products to deceive buyers. It is really unscrupulous and destroys the vitality of domestic goods, and should be thoroughly investigated to warn against traitors. According to the previous letter, in addition to separate letters, the original attached notice is enclosed and sent for your reference, and all members should pay attention to it and must not be negligent.

Important Notice from the Felt Hat Industry

Respectfully, it is found that our country's industry is backward, which leads to the flooding of foreign goods in the market. Just taking our felt hats as an example, the number of imports each year is no less than 1.5 million yuan. In recent years, the Chinese people have been aware of this and have worked hard to resist it, hoping to stop the leaks. Unexpectedly, at this time of rapid advancement, some merchants who disregard the overall situation have ordered large quantities of inferior goods and sold them on the market under the name of a certain foreign firm to seek meager profits. There are also unscrupulous merchants who add trademarks and labels to inferior felt hats and call them domestic products. All kinds of work to change the face is perfect, so that the domestic felt hat industry is destroyed. Inferior goods are mixed with genuine goods, and they can take the opportunity to import. If we do not rectify the situation and find ways to prevent it, the future of domestic felt hats will have no foothold, and even the national economy and people's livelihood will be greatly affected. The trade association has gathered 17 members of felt hat factories in Shanghai to actively carry out and properly find solutions. First, the trademarks of the 17 companies were published in the newspaper, and letters were sent to party and government organs and business associations and domestic goods associations in various provinces for verification. Afterwards, if any manufacturer has the above-mentioned counterfeiting or代製 and other circumstances, once verified, in addition to publishing a notice in the newspaper, we will request the party and government organs in various provinces to strictly punish them, and the domestic goods organizations to jointly publicize. I am especially worried that when the people of the country purchase and use them, they will not be able to distinguish them and will be deceived. The trademarks of the 17 manufacturers that manufacture genuine domestic felt hats are listed in detail below for easy reference. I hope that patriots will share their wisdom.

Ministry of the Interior Changes the Method of Issuing Physician Certificates

Approved by the National Physicians Association

The National Physicians Association previously stated that the Ministry of Health's Provisional Regulations for Physicians and the Legislative Yuan's revised Regulations for Western Physicians were difficult to implement and out of date, and the association repeatedly requested amendments. It is now heard that the Ministry of the Interior's Department of Health has drafted two temporary measures for the issuance of certificates to physicians, which were submitted to the Executive Yuan and approved at the 49th meeting on July 12. The amended regulations and the public letter from the Ministry of the Interior's Department of Health to the association are as follows: [Respectfully, according to the files in the case, we previously approved your association's letter, stating that there is a shortage of physicians and requesting that we follow the precedents of advanced countries and start with leniency, etc. Now, our department has drafted two temporary measures for the issuance of certificates: (1) Graduates of unapproved medical schools who have graduated for more than four years, and whose school's curriculum and facilities have been examined and deemed perfect by this department, and who graduated before the promulgation of the Provisional Regulations for Physicians in the 18th year; (2) Those who have been recognized by this department as having perfect facilities. Hospitals, practicing for more than five years, and who have been practicing before the 18th year, have been issued a medical license or certificate by the competent authorities in the place where they are located, and have proven to have the ability to practice medicine, and have been verified to be free of differences, will be temporarily allowed to issue certificates once only, and no precedents will be set in the future, which will be reported by the department to the Executive Yuan for approval and implementation. It has now been proposed by the Executive Yuan at the 49th meeting this month and resolved and approved. In addition to the Ministry issuing orders to various provinces and cities to specifically order them to handle the matter, and issuing separate letters, a corresponding letter is hereby sent to inform you that we hope you will investigate and be informed.], etc.

Northeast Telegrams Have Long Been Blocked

Zhong E Talks About the So-Called Blockade

Regarding the issue of Northeast telecommunications, since the September 18th Incident, it has been almost entirely plundered by the Japanese, leading to rumors that our side will implement a blockade of Northeast telecommunications. A reporter from Xinsheng News Agency interviewed Zhong E, the director of the Telecommunications Department, yesterday. According to him, Northeast telecommunications can be divided into wired and wireless. Wired telecommunications are directly under the control of the central government, while wireless telecommunications are mostly for military use and are directly managed by the Northeast authorities. After the September 18th Incident, our telecommunications were seized by the Japanese. Wireless telecommunications cannot be communicated, and wired telecommunications, except for the Commercial Daily, cannot be communicated. Even if there are reports, they must be forwarded from Tianjin to Harbin and then sent to various places. Whether or not they are intercepted on the way and can directly reach is still not guaranteed. All countries communicate with the Northeast after the September 18th Incident. Our side has protested to them and asked them to stop communicating. Various countries maintain the old contract and do not communicate with the puppet state with a new treaty. However, the puppet state is definitely not the legitimate successor of China and cannot continue the old contract. Our diplomatic authorities are already negotiating. Most of our telecommunications personnel in the Northeast have returned to Guan Nei. Under such circumstances, the relationship with the puppet state has been severed invisibly, and there is no so-called blockade. As for the issue of the circulation of the Commercial Daily, although there is no major obstacle, in order to be cautious, the Ministry of Communications has specially asked the Telecommunications Department to study which Commercial Dailies can circulate and which Commercial Dailies cannot. There is still no result.

The Extra-Territorial Road Construction Case Will Be Discussed Again Next Wednesday Is Incorrect

Secretary-General Yu's Talk

Regarding the issue of extra-territorial road construction, it was reported in the newspaper yesterday that Feixin Dun, the director-general of the Public Works Bureau, will meet with Secretary-General of the Municipal Government Yu Hongjun again next Wednesday to continue the discussion. A reporter from the Central News Agency asked Secretary-General Yu about this matter yesterday. According to Yu's reply to the reporter, he has not heard of continuing the discussion next Wednesday. During the recess of the Board of Directors of the Public Works Bureau, he will continue to discuss the matter. As of tonight (that is, last night), he has not received a notice from Feixin Dun. The reporter also learned from another source that the main body for resolving the extra-territorial road construction this time is the Municipal Government and the Public Works Bureau. The Public Works Bureau submitted the draft agreement on the case to the consular corps only because the case is also closely related to foreign residents, so it followed the example of submitting the draft agreement to the consular corps to solicit its opinion. The Public Works Bureau is only responsible to all taxpayers and has no direct relationship with the consular corps. Therefore, the agreement on the recovery of extra-territorial road construction does not need to be approved by the consular corps.

Opinions on the Abolition of Taels and the Adoption of Yuan in Various Industries

The New Currency Must Have a Moderate Price

The Conversion Ratio Should Be Publicly Determined

Public Inspection and Supervision of Issuance

The Sugar Industry Association and other associations replied to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, saying: "Respectfully, we have received your letter asking about the three questions regarding the abolition of taels and the adoption of yuan. Since the Han and Tang dynasties, there has never been a complete and unified system of currency in our country. The five-zhu and three-zhu leather coins and paper money were extremely chaotic. The Qing Dynasty had its own minting, and the quality was inconsistent, so the credibility was different. Since the Revolution, the provinces have been in power, the number of minting institutions has increased, and the types of currency have become more and more complicated. Even if the land is adjacent, the suggestion of abolishing taels and adopting yuan to unify the currency system has been advocated for 15 years. However, it has not been realized due to frequent political changes, which is a pity in public opinion. At this time when the price of li is plummeting and the industry and commerce are feeling the dark losses, the policy of abolishing taels and adopting yuan is even more of an urgent plan for the social people. However, things in the world are often beneficial and harmful, so at the beginning of the reform, we must consider carefully and not rush to do things. Recently, people in the financial industry and economists have discussed this issue. Although there are differences in opinions, the principle of eliminating abuses must be a common opinion of all sectors. I am honored to be consulted, and I will offer some humble opinions as far as I can see, which may also be welcomed by the wise public of your association. The first point of the letter is about the fineness and weight of the new currency. Liu Hongsheng and Geng Aide in the research association have expressed their views. However, the three must meet the moderate price of the current old currency of the foreign li. If it is too high, the new currency will be eliminated, and if it is too low, the production price will be easily affected. Fortunately, the Ministry of Finance has already stated that it will never seek profit in the minting factory. This is what we hope that your association and the social people will supervise the government from beginning to end and fulfill the promise. The second point is about the ratio of silver contracts to silver coins. Except for the major trading ports along the coast of the Yangtze River, there are few cases where silver units are used to sign contracts. In the inland market, it can be said that there are very few. Therefore, the ratio of silver contracts to silver coins during the current effective period may solicit the opinions of both debtors to determine a transitional method. This is what we hope that your association will convene the Silver Money Association and related industries to properly determine a method. In view of this change, if you want the society and the public to understand and trust it, this depends on the government's prestige. No one dares to affirm it in turn. Today's doubts about the government are nothing more than a few points, such as worrying about no preparation, no ability to unify the right to issue, indiscriminately minting inferior coins, indiscriminately issuing banknotes, concentrating cash, and suddenly stopping redemption. These kinds of malpractices do have the need to worry about. The government authorities, if they sincerely want the society and the public to understand and trust them, then they should ask themselves and take precautions in advance. If the minting of hard currency must be made public to see whether the quality is accurate, and the issuance of banknotes must be publicly inspected to see whether the preparation is sufficient, unify the minting institutions and eliminate the occurrence of inferior coins. All of these points are waiting for your association to lead the business community, organize a supervisory agency, and urge its implementation. In short, the change of the monetary system belongs to the scope of national administration, and it may be implemented on a regular basis with a single order. Only because it is a major plan for the reform of social and economic development, we should not hesitate to consult extensively and aim for perfection. If the above-mentioned sections can be linked together and determined, then the policy of abolishing taels and adopting yuan to unify the monetary system will be promoted to the greatest benefit. Otherwise, a slight mistake will lead to a great difference. If the benefit is not seen, abuses will have sprung up. Is this what the society and the public are happy to hear? The letter is sent to you for the above reasons, and we hope that you will check it out. This is addressed to the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce, the Sugar Industry, the Cotton Cloth Industry, the Rice Store Industry, the Silk Brocade Industry, the North-South Goods Exchange Industry, the Mercerized Cotton Weaving Industry, the Color Printing Industry, the Mineral Ash Factory Industry, the Fly Ash Industry, and the Intestine Industry Association. August 1."

Establishment of a Medical Bureau in Zhuanqiao Town

Zhuanqiao Town, located west of Shanghai and spanning the Songjiang and Shanghai counties, is relatively developed in commerce due to its convenient transportation. The local gentry, Zhou Yue and He Qiu, considering the years of famine and the devastation of the people's livelihood, and especially the likelihood of a major epidemic after a large-scale military conflict, and that many residents in the vicinity were suffering from illness but were unable to afford medical treatment due to economic hardship, in order to promote social well-being, jointly organized a medical bureau with Lu Faxin and Ma Youliang from the Zhuanqiao Town Office in the Fourth District of Songjiang County. They invited more than 20 renowned doctors to provide medical treatment starting from the third day of the sixth lunar month at the Zhenqiao Primary School, which served as the bureau's location. The schedule was set for the 3rd and 8th days of each month, and each session attracted over a thousand patients. Free medicine was provided to the poor and sick. The original plan was to end after six sessions, but due to the large number of patients seeking treatment, it was necessary to extend the period. With the consent of the doctors, it was decided to extend it for two more sessions, ending on the eighth day of the seventh lunar month.

Shanghai Public Utilities Bureau Supervises the Repair of Wusong River Ferries

Five Ferries Repaired

Commendation Issued

There are a total of thirteen privately-operated ferries on the Wusong River in this city. They used to use ordinary barges to carry passengers. The Municipal Public Utilities Bureau registered them in the 18th year [of the Republic, i.e., 1929] and reorganized them. All ferries were required to build new boats according to the specified drawings. The following year, they were ordered by the Public Utilities Bureau to add auxiliary boats as backup and to increase the number of trips when passengers were crowded. After the war this year, when the ferries resumed operation, the bureau found that except for one at Tanziwan, the paint on the other ferries was peeling off and the boats were dilapidated. They were ordered to repair and repaint them to maintain their appearance and avoid danger. It is now learned that the five ferries at Tongji Road, Hanzhong Road, Guangzhao Road, Guangfu Road, and Panjiawan have been repaired as ordered. The bureau sent personnel to inspect them and found that the ten main and auxiliary ferries, both inside and outside, the paint on the railings and the awning supports were clean and in good condition. The bureau believes that the ferry operators have earnestly complied with the city's regulations on ferries over the years and have contributed greatly to improving transportation. Therefore, they have been issued commendations.

Shen Jitu Accused of Abandoning Wife for Concubine

His Wife Makes Four Demands

Shen Jitu, son of Shen Qiquan, a former Qing Dynasty scholar, married Ms. Huang Zhaohua in the 12th year of the Republic [i.e., 1923] through the matchmaking of Zhang Yipeng and Huang Yanpei. At first, their relationship was harmonious, and Huang gave birth to a daughter the following year. However, after Shen Jitu entered officialdom, he repeatedly obtained favorable positions, accumulated wealth, and became increasingly wealthy. He then built a gilded cage to keep a concubine for his pleasure, gradually becoming indifferent to his wife. This spring, when the anti-Japanese war broke out in Shanghai, Jitu was residing on the sea, but he only took his beloved concubine with him to the Jing'an Villa, abandoning his legal wife. Later, although Huang tried to join him, he refused to let her in, practicing the principle of "when disaster strikes, each flies his own way." At that time, Huang was pregnant and almost died of anger. Fortunately, her father was by her side and felt that Jitu's behavior was unreasonable. He decided not to argue with him for the time being and first persuaded his daughter to leave and stay at the Qianji Hotel for medical treatment. Later, he began to negotiate with Jitu, but he ignored him and treated him like a stranger. Now, Huang's illness has been cured, but she is about to give birth, and it is not a long-term solution to continue wandering. Therefore, she hired attorney Xuan Zhendong to file a petition with the First Special District Court, requesting mediation. However, Shen Jitu failed to appear in court, and the mediation could not proceed. Huang then officially filed a lawsuit, requesting the court to order the defendant to pay: (1) 40 yuan per month for living expenses from February 1st of this year, calculated for ten years, totaling 4,800 yuan. In addition, 1,000 yuan for childbirth expenses and the child's living expenses. (2) Return the plaintiff's clothes and utensils. (3) Return the adopted daughter, Nannan, whom the plaintiff brought. (4) Order the defendant to bear the litigation costs. Yesterday morning, Judge Shen Hong opened the court to summon the defendant, but he still did not appear. The plaintiff, Huang Luhua, stated that she was 25 years old and currently residing at No. 15, Guanhua Lane, Lafayette Road. The defendant, Shen Jitu, had previously served in Anchang, Yidong, and other customs positions and is now a county magistrate. It is said that he has gone to Shaanxi on official business. In the past, he used to give 10 to 20 yuan of pocket money per month, but he has not given any money recently. The daughter I gave birth to died early, while the concubine has two daughters and one son. After the defendant's attorney and the plaintiff's attorney debated with each other, the judge ordered a change of date for further verification.

Not a Factory Girl, but a Bride

Husband Follows Behind and Realizes the Truth

Rickshaw puller Wang Deyi from Taixian, whose wife Wang Wang, 22 years old, is attractive. Recently, due to financial difficulties, Wang Wang planned to work in a factory. Gu San and Zhu Jin acted as introducers, claiming to introduce her to work at the pig farm on Yidingpan Road. They took her there three times to make contact, but each time they said the manager was not there. The day before yesterday, they came to Wang's house again, saying the manager wanted to see her. Wang Wang changed her clothes and went out with them. Wang Deyi saw his wife dressed up and realized it was not like going to work, so he secretly followed behind. Unexpectedly, they went to Wang Nanting's house near the pig farm, and there were already many people gathered at the door, saying they were there to see the bride. Wang Nanting's house was in a state of celebration. At this point, Wang Deyi realized that his wife had been sold. He immediately called the police, and Gu, Zhu, and Wang Nanting were arrested in the Sixth District. Yesterday, they were sent to court for investigation.

Page 15

Local News

Reconsideration of Dismissed Cases

Cases where reconsideration requests have been rejected by a higher authority cannot be appealed to a higher authority. Wang Zhennan, Chief Prosecutor of the Second Branch of the Jiangsu High Court, recently received an order from the Prosecutor's Office of the Supreme Court regarding reconsideration requests. There have been slight changes recently, and he has been ordered to comply and inform the public. Therefore, Chief Prosecutor Wang issued a notice yesterday, as follows: Notice to all parties. The Prosecutor's Office of the Supreme Court has forwarded an instruction from the Judicial Yuan of the National Government, stating that regarding reconsideration requests, the interpretation of laws has been unified through a meeting, and the interpretation has been changed. If a complainant is dissatisfied with the decision of a prosecutor in the court of first instance not to prosecute and requests reconsideration, after the chief prosecutor of the higher court rejects the request, he may not request reconsideration from the chief prosecutor of a higher court. It is ordered to inform and instruct the subordinates to comply, and to inform all parties concerned. This order, etc. Upon receipt, in addition to forwarding, it is ordered to inform the chief prosecutor and instruct the subordinates to comply, and to inform all complainants. This notice.

One-Year Imprisonment for Seducing a Female Worker

Yang Simei, a woman from Pudong, 19 years old, worked as a female worker at the Yihe Cotton Mill on Yangshupu Road. In April of this year, she was stalked, seduced and made fun of by Xie Ada, a rascal from Jiangbei, who waited near the entrance of the cotton mill every day after work. Yang, from Pudong, had little experience and was thus charmed. On the 27th, the two of them went to Wuxi together and rented a house at No. 5 Guangqin Road, where they lived together as husband and wife. However, Yang's travel expenses were limited. After living there for about a week, she ran out of money. Shen Zhang, a woman who lived in the same house, told Yang to return to Shanghai because Xie Ada planned to take Yang to Fujian to sell her. Therefore, Yang insisted on forcing Xie to return to Shanghai on May 24th. Because she was ashamed to go home, she stayed temporarily at her relatives' place at No. 19 Tongzhou Road. Yang Shunjin, her father, opened a burlap sack store in Pudong. After his daughter disappeared, he searched for her everywhere. He had previously received a report from a friend surnamed Mou, saying that he had seen Yang Simei in Wuxi and that she had returned to Shanghai. The morning before yesterday, Yang Shunjin met his daughter on Wuzhou Road, learned the details, and reported it together to the Jiaxing Road Police Station. The head of the report, Liu Junjie, was sent to arrest Xie Ada and bring him to the police station. The next morning, he was sent to the Fourth Criminal Court of the First Special District Court. The police lawyer Zhang Tianyin stated the case and said that the defendant had previously been prosecuted for flirting with his daughter, and therefore requested severe punishment. Subsequently, Yang Simei and her father, Yang Shunjin, explained the details of the incident and questioned the defendant. He stammered in his confession and claimed that Yang Simei was introduced to him by his cousin and that it cost him dozens of silver dollars, and that it was not seduction. Judge Chuan Lin examined the confession clearly and declared to the defendant that he did not need to argue and sentenced Xie Ada to one year of imprisonment to deter others. Yang Simei was returned to her father for custody.

Private Possession of Sulfur Punished

Dingyu Seafood Store at No. 38 of a foreign firm in the French Concession was found to be privately storing the banned substance sulfur by the Jiangsu Provincial Nitre and Sulfur Branch Office for Special Districts. The director of the bureau sent Yang Yucheng, the head of the business department, to report to the French Concession Police. Detective Jin Mingxiang was sent to search the store and found 14 catties of sulfur, along with the store clerk Chen Shumei. They were taken to the police station and sent to the Second Special District Court. The police prosecuted them for the public danger crime under Article 201 of the Criminal Law. Chen confessed that he had bought it last year and used it to whiten white fungus. He also hired a lawyer to defend him. The trial was concluded, and yesterday Judge Xiong Huiping presided over the First Criminal Court and sentenced Chen Shumei for the crime of assisting in the unauthorized possession of explosives and specially fined him 120 yuan. If he could not pay the fine, he would be imprisoned for one day for every two yuan. The number of days of detention before the judgment was finalized would be offset by two yuan per day. The sulfur was confiscated.

Morphine Hidden in Luggage

Turns Out It Wasn't Weapons

The Shanghai Garrison Command recently received a tip that multiple packages of pawned luggage from Yutaiyi Pawnshop were stored in the cargo room of the Shanghai-Hangzhou Railway South Station. It was alleged that a large amount of weapons was hidden inside and entrusted to the Public Welfare Transportation Company for transportation to Hangzhou to support bandits. After learning about the above situation, the Command sent Inspector Yang Bin to the South Station at 6 PM the night before last to inspect the cargo warehouse together with the Railway Police Department. Since the iron gates of the cargo warehouse were locked that night, the Railway Police Department temporarily detained the cargo. At 12 PM yesterday, Yang Bin, the inspector of the Command, led detectives and soldiers to the South Station to jointly inspect the cargo with Zhang Shuping, the deputy director of the Railway Police Department, Zhou Fusheng, the stationmaster of the Transportation Department, cargo inspectors, and Liu Shaoqing, the foreman of the Detective Team of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, and Liu Xueli, the patrol chief of the Second District Police Station. Because the smuggling of weapons to support bandits was a serious matter, soldiers of the Command were heavily armed around the cargo room of the station. As a result, four clothing packages from Hengfeng Pawnshop, four from Yufeng Pawnshop, one from Yutai Pawnshop, and four from Yutaiyi Pawnshop were seized. A large amount of morphine weighing seven kilograms was seized from the Yutaiyi clothing packages, divided into five silk bags and two cloth bags, with a total weight of more than 120 taels, worth approximately 3,000 yuan. Each of the other clothing packages contained a large number of inferior goods, leather goods, and cloth, but no weapons. The Command sent the four Yutai clothing packages and Ke Lizhi, the clerk of the pawnshop, to the Command for interrogation, along with the morphine. The other clothing packages contained more than a dozen pieces of leather goods, which were declared as fourth-class goods and transported at fourth-class freight rates. The railway authorities believed that according to the regulations, leather goods must be charged at first-class freight rates, so they considered it a case of fraud and detained all the clothing packages of the pawnshops, ordering the cargo owners to pay the supplementary fine according to the regulations. The item of inferior goods must be submitted for review.

Extortion in Connection with Assassination

Claiming to be a Government Official, Swindling Money, Zhong Liansong Reports to the Police to Arrest the Criminal

Cao Qing, an inspector of the Shanghai Municipal Public Security Bureau, was assassinated by thugs on Carre Road in the French Concession. Director Wen recently received a confidential report from citizen Chen Er, stating that the main culprit in the case was Zhong Liansong, who is now a foreman in the telephone bureau in the Concession. Director Wen instructed the Inspection Department to investigate the case thoroughly. On the 30th of last month, a man suddenly came to Zhong Liansong's house on Hanzhong Road in Zhabei, claiming to be Shen Bin, an investigator in a certain bureau. Zhong invited him in, and Shen said that the Detective Team of the Public Security Bureau wanted to arrest him because he was the main culprit in the assassination of Inspector Cao. If he was arrested, his life would be in danger. Shen said that he was not bragging and that he had evidence to prove it. He handed over a letter from a certain person reporting to a certain bureau. The letter stated that Zhong was the main culprit in the assassination. Zhong was shocked and replied that he was a legitimate worker and would never do such a thing. He asked Shen not to misunderstand. Shen said that it was no use, as people were accusing him. He asked how he could deal with it. Shen said that he knew that Zhong was a good person, so he came to inform him. Zhong repeatedly begged Shen to find a way to intercede with the Public Security Bureau to avoid his arrest. Shen agreed immediately and arranged to meet at the Little World Amusement Park in the city at around 9 PM the next night. Because he had mistakenly identified Zhong's face, he told Zhong to carry a flashlight as proof when he went. Zhong agreed. Shen then left. Afterwards, Zhong realized that Shen was clearly trying to extort money, so he reported it to the Detective Team of the Municipal Public Security Bureau and asked them to arrest him. Because the matter involved impersonating a public official and extorting money, Detective Wang Shenqing, along with the police chief of the First District Second Police Station, disguised themselves as coolies and went to the Little World Amusement Park at around 8 PM. Zhong took a flashlight and went to the amusement park to keep the appointment. Before long, Shen came leisurely. After they greeted each other, they began to negotiate. Shen said that he needed 300 yuan to withdraw the case and prevent Zhong from being arrested. Zhong pretended to negotiate and reduce the amount, and at the same time scratched his head wildly (this was a pre-arranged signal with the detectives). At that moment, the detectives who were lying in ambush in the four places rushed forward, arrested Shen, and took him to the Second Police Station of the First District for questioning.

Central Bank Inspection Report

132nd Time

The 132nd Central Bank Issuance Reserve Inspection Report states: According to the provisions of Article 15 of the Central Bank Ordinance, this committee is responsible for inspecting the reserve for the issuance of convertible notes of this bank. On July 30, 1932, Supervisor Qin Runqing conducted the 132nd inspection at the Issuance Bureau of this bank. The results of the inspection are hereby announced as follows: (A) The total amount of convertible notes issued is 29,529,531 silver dollars, including 26,566,804 silver dollar notes and 2,962,727 subsidiary currency notes. The total amount of the convertible note reserve is 29,529,531 silver dollars, including 24,055,531 silver dollars in cash reserve. This cash reserve includes 21,472,040.74 silver dollars stored in the issuance vault of this bank, 1,411,305 silver dollars stored in branches in various ports, and 1,172,185.26 silver dollars stored with other banks. The guarantee reserve is equivalent to 5,474,000 silver dollars. (B) The total amount of customs gold convertible notes issued is 377,089.40 yuan. The total amount of the customs gold convertible note reserve is 377,089.40 yuan. This reserve includes 4,201 taels, 4 qian, and 9 fen of gold, stored in the issuance vault of this bank, at a fixed price of 60 to convert 252,089.40 yuan of customs gold, and 50,000 US dollars, stored with other banks in this port, at a fixed price of 40 to convert 125,000 yuan of customs gold. According to Article 2 of the Central Bank Convertible Note Regulations, the cash reserve is 60% and the guarantee reserve is 40%. The results of this inspection show that the cash reserve exceeds 60% and the guarantee reserve is less than 40%, which is in accordance with the regulations. This report is hereby made. July 30, 1932, Central Bank Supervisory Board.

Injures Customer...Authorities Punish

The Zhoudeji Barber Shop at the intersection of Mingguo Road, Guanyin Street, and Baojiang Alley in the city had a light bulb fall and injure a customer's head the other day. The Municipal Public Utilities Bureau sent personnel to investigate after receiving a report. Record of the General Meeting of Tenants in Yuqing and Qixiu Neighborhoods

The tenants of Yuqing and Qixiu neighborhoods on North Sichuan Road held a general membership meeting yesterday morning at 9:00 AM. Over two hundred people attended, with Zhang Chiseng of the Shanghai Citizens' Rent Reduction Committee present. The meeting was chaired by Jiang Wenbao, and formalities were observed. (A) Wei Langxuan reported on the progress of negotiations. (B) Discussions included: (1) How to handle the exemption of rent in war zones. A resolution was passed in principle. (2) The issue of organizing a special committee. It was resolved to appoint seven people, including Jiang Wenbao, to be responsible for conducting negotiations. (3) Given that this neighborhood is at the forefront of the conflict, in a particularly dangerous and precarious area, with massive casualties and losses, and that housing repairs will not be completed until early June, with tenants only returning to settle in July, it was resolved that rent payments should begin in August. (4) The issue of the management office taking advantage of the situation to exert pressure, such as filing lawsuits for rent arrears. It was resolved that all members would stand united to achieve their goals, sharing the costs of legal representation. The minimum demand is for rent exemption starting from July. (5) What to do if the management office sends personnel to forcibly collect rent for May, June, and July. It was resolved to inspect the rent receipts and pay according to whether they are for August or July; otherwise, to refuse payment collectively and deposit the rent for July and August into a bank to avoid accusations of rent arrears. (6) As the houses in Qixiu neighborhood are still under construction and not yet completed, it was resolved that the start of rent collection should not be treated the same as other areas, and the matter was entrusted to a special committee. (7) Zhang Chiseng, representative of the Municipal Rent Reduction Committee, provided guidance, with the wording omitted here for brevity. The meeting adjourned with tea and refreshments at noon.

News on the Rent Dispute in Chongshan Neighborhood, Tangshan Road

Previously, the tenants of Chongshan Neighborhood argued that the rent rates had increased several times after the renovation of the neighborhood. Following the Shanghai Incident, all industries declined, and even with frugality, tenants were struggling to make ends meet, making the high rent unaffordable. Therefore, they collectively decided to write to the landlord, earnestly requesting a reduction or exemption of rent as relief. Unexpectedly, the landlord not only showed no sympathy but also filed a lawsuit for rent arrears in the First Special District Local Court. Upon investigation, the neighborhood was only renovated and completed in mid-April of this year. The landlord had verbally agreed that rent would start in May, and tenants had prepaid one month's rent at the time of the agreement. The outstanding rent for June was deposited in the bank because the landlord refused to reduce the rent as requested. Therefore, this case is purely about rent reduction and not a dispute over arrears. The case was heard twice on July 26th and 29th. The judge, considering the complexity of the rent reduction issue, briefly questioned the plaintiff's name and then instructed the tenants' lawyer, Guo Qiming, to gather evidence for a scheduled rehearing. Currently, the tenants are not only appealing to all sectors for assistance but also collecting evidence to argue their case reasonably. During the previous hearing, many residents from Tangshan Road and the surrounding areas went to the courtroom to observe. It is certain that the next hearing will be even more crowded than before because the matter concerns housing, which is a pressing issue for all.

British and American Workers Request Cancellation of Factory Management Rules

The authorities of the British American Tobacco Company in this city formulated 23 articles of factory management rules this year, which have been implemented since the first of last month. Workers in both the new and old factories of the company in Pudong consider these rules extremely harsh. For example, laughing or speaking in the factory will result in one demerit and one day of suspension. In addition to deducting meal expenses, one demerit will also be recorded. There are many other offenses that lead to demerits. Accumulating three demerits results in one major demerit, and accumulating three major demerits leads to dismissal. Furthermore, the most severe rule is that the factory has the right to dismiss workers at will. Therefore, the workers believe that not only is it extremely difficult to work in the factory, but they also lose their inherent protection. This treatment is even harsher than during the warlord era, and they can no longer endure it. They have been going to the Fifth District Cigarette Industry Union to question the reasons for the Social Affairs Bureau's approval and demand that the rules be canceled. After several discussions, the union believes that these harsh rules contradict the Factory Law and the labor-management mutual assistance agreement signed between the union and the factory in 1927. It has decided to convene an emergency meeting of all representatives from both factories on the afternoon of the 4th of this month to discuss countermeasures.

Mail

Basic Principles of Railway Transportation Regulations

(Continued) Zheng Baozhao

Those who only engage in the business of forwarding goods should not be considered common carriers. From a legal perspective, express delivery companies complete the actual transportation business through their agents and collect freight charges. As for the forwarder, they do not receive the benefit of freight charges and do not actually transport the goods. Based on this distinction, the former is a common carrier, while the latter is not.

Most legal scholars believe that sleeping car companies are not common carriers. They themselves do not transport passengers, but only provide passengers with sleeping facilities. Passengers purchase tickets from the railway, and the railway uses the sleeping car company's vehicles to actually transport passengers. Therefore, the railway must bear the responsibility of a common carrier. (X) Insurer's Responsibility and Baggage Transportation. According to ordinary rules, a common carrier has no obligation to transport goods using passenger cars. However, in practice, carriers often assume the obligation to transport passengers' baggage within a considerable stipulated weight. This business is not considered uncompensated because the fare is already included in the ticket price. Baggage transportation is part of freight transportation, so the legal restrictions it is subject to must also be within the scope of the carrier's obligation to transport baggage, assuming the responsibility of all insurers of common carriers and being liable for the loss of baggage. Therefore, what can be considered baggage transportation is a prerequisite for resolving baggage transportation liability. A detailed description is given below: (A) Items for personal convenience and need can be considered baggage transportation. All items related to the personal convenience and needs of passengers during the trip can be considered baggage transportation. If it exceeds the amount and value of this convenience and need, it cannot be considered baggage. (B) Items related to the passenger's occupation can also be considered baggage transportation. All items that passengers carry that are necessary for their occupation, such as the knives and saws carried by carpenters. If such items carried by passengers are lost, the carrier must bear the responsibility of an insurer. (C) Goods cannot be considered baggage transportation. Because in ordinary circumstances, carriers acknowledge that items for the convenience and needs of passengers can be transported as baggage, they can refuse to transport items beyond this scope as baggage. They can only be changed to freight transport or transported by passenger car with additional freight charges. Now, if a passenger submits a batch of items to the railway for baggage transportation, of which 90% are goods, and does not declare the nature of the contents to the railway, then the railway does not bear the responsibility of a common carrier. Because the railway is not subject to the legal restrictions of recognizing goods as baggage transportation after the contents of the goods are disclosed, if it is carried, there is no insurer's liability. (D) Goods of obvious nature. If the nature of the contents of the goods submitted by the passenger is extremely obvious and there is no concealment, if the carrier receives it as baggage transportation, then it must bear the responsibility of all insurers of common carriers. Because the goods have not been mixed up or disguised as baggage, the railway could have charged for it as freight transportation. Now that it has been negligent and transported it as baggage, it must be held liable for damages in the same way as freight transportation.

(XI) The question of whether the right of possession remains in the hands of the owner. The reasons why common carriers bear the responsibility of insurance have been described in detail above, because the carrier has absolute management and possession of the goods in transit, and the owner has no way of obtaining evidence of the carrier's errors. Therefore, if the carrier is not entrusted by the merchant to manage and keep the goods on their behalf, it is not liable as an insurer. Therefore, the right to keep and manage the items carried by passengers is in their own hands, so if there is a loss, the railway is not liable.

(III) The responsibility of common carriers to provide fair services and collect reasonable fares.

Now, let us try to explain the obligations and responsibilities of common carriers from the perspective of common law.

(1) Fair carriage of goods. Carriers must treat all merchants fairly and equally. This is also considered a matter of course in common law. If a carrier refuses the goods of Party A while unconditionally carrying the goods of Party B, it is considered an illegal act. Because this kind of behavior is enough to create a special position for one party, help it monopolize the formation of patents, and at the same time harm the business of its competitors. In other words, the railway must be responsible for transporting the goods of any merchant, and all carriage and delivery methods must not be different or discriminatory. This obligation is the inherent duty of the carrier and is also a necessary policy for public utilities. The reason why railways must treat the public fairly is that the government has given them various privileges, and this is precisely what is hoped for.

(2) Fair supply of vehicles. Carriers have an obligation to fairly distribute all equipment. If they go against this, it will inevitably lead to extremely serious differential treatment. Because if the supply of vehicles for a certain shipper is very fast, and the vehicles needed by its competitors are forced to wait, then the latter's favorable market will inevitably be lost, and its goods will rot or suffer other major damage. If the railway has promised to allocate a certain number of vehicles to a merchant's request, but is unable to supply the full number due to practical difficulties at that time, then the merchant may not protest. Only by notifying the railway with a rational attitude and asking it to make every effort to allocate the vehicles as soon as possible within the possible range, and without hindering the previous requests of other shippers at the same station and affecting the business of other sections of the line, can the request be made. Railways must treat shippers at all stations along the line equally. No station, in other words, no merchant, may force the railway to disregard the interests of other stations or merchants and provide itself with full convenience.

Supplement to the Local Edition of Shenbao

Words

"A Solution Exists"

— Buddha

The words "a solution exists" are most welcome to my ears, because the worst thing in the world is not having a solution. If a solution exists, there is no problem. However, is the so-called "solution" just a verbal one or an actual one? I have had two impressions of the so-called "solution."

Previously, I saw that the business of a certain store was not going well and it was about to close down. As a result, creditors gathered to demand payment upon hearing the news. The store stated, "Please rest assured, everyone. We have a solution, and we will certainly satisfy your expectations in the shortest amount of time." But when the time came, it had already closed its doors and declared bankruptcy. The creditors wandered outside the door, without any recourse, and had to entrust a lawyer to recover the debt. This is one example of "a solution exists." I also saw several gentlemen on the road, flexing their muscles and glaring at each other with hatred. First, there was an argument, then violence. As a result, A won and B lost. B had no way to retaliate, and pointed at A, saying, "Be careful. I've suffered a loss at your hands today, but I definitely won't let you go. I have my own solution. Be careful." This is also an example of "a solution exists."

Yesterday, I saw the results of the Pingzheng Committee meeting, which stated that "a solution exists" for the military situation in Rehe. I am suspicious.

Arts and Culture

Words of Awakening

— Songfu

Rumors abound, causing residents to flee in panic. There is no safe haven within the country now. Where is the peaceful and happy land?

Which is better, British or Chinese rule? Do not advocate for confusing people's minds. I advise the people not to disturb themselves and to be content with their fate.

Where do you want to go in this thorny land? It is too late to regret wasting money. Property is ultimately an external possession. Only your heart knows the gains and losses of survival and death.

Monsters arise from humans; there is no need to worry. Live in peace and do not worry unnecessarily. From now on, stop listening to rumors and do not let villains succeed in their schemes.

Science

Method of Making Alkali from Wood Ash

— Er Cheng

Before the advent of soap, rural women used grass ash soaked in water to wash clothes, which certainly had the ability to remove dirt. However, its use was very inconvenient. Modern science has made great progress, and it has been found that the ability of grass ash to remove dirt is entirely due to the alkaline substances it contains, such as Potassium Carbonate (M2CO3), which are the main dirt-removing raw materials for industrial and household use, and are also the basic raw materials for making caustic potash. These alkalis can be extracted from wood ash. Now, I will record this method below, which is also a method of waste utilization.

Raw material - Rice straw forest ash

Method - If we want to make alkali, the first thing is to choose the raw material. Although all grass and wood ash contain potassium, the amount they contain is different. Generally, grass ash contains more potassium than wood ash, and bark ash contains more than trunk ash, so it is most appropriate to use grass ash to make alkali. However, it is more important to note that once the grass and wood are completely burned, the ash turns white, and the amount of potassium it contains is lost. Therefore, it is best to take rice straw ash that is not completely burned and has a black color. Once the choice of raw material is determined, it can be prepared for manufacturing.

First, take a wooden barrel with a hole in the side of the bottom, and plug it with a cork. Cover the bottom with two or three layers of thin cloth, then put the grass and wood ash into the barrel, and soak it in clean water for a day and night. At first, it must be gradually stirred, and then let it stand. Then, pull out the cork, and the liquid will flow out of the hole, and the residue will remain in the barrel, which can be used as fertilizer. Put the ash quality that flows out into a pot, and heat it over a low heat. When the water evaporates, you can add more ash juice. Evaporate it gradually, and the liquid in the pot gradually becomes thicker. Then, you can take out a small amount in a bowl and let it cool. If it can solidify, then remove the pot from the heat and let it cool. Then, you will see a yellow crude alkali forming. This yellow crude alkali is very impure. It is best to refine it. The method of refining is to dissolve the crude alkali in clean water, stir it slowly, and let it stand for a day or two. Take the clear liquid on top and cook it in the same way as before. Then, you will see a white, pure alkali precipitate.

Fashion

A Modern Woman I Know

— Shao Guang

Among the several female friends I know, only Miss Wang has left the deepest impression on me. Indeed, she truly deserves to be called a thoroughly modernized contemporary woman. However, she likes to say in front of people, "I am a modern and artistic woman, a representative of the surging tide of modern times." Therefore, I can only refer to her as a modern and artistic (?) woman. She is a product of Shanghai. Because she is a product of Shanghai, she is thoroughly modern. As for art, standing on a truly non-artistic point of view, one can also call it complete.

So, how modern is Miss Wang? — Artistry is really out of the question. Yes, as long as you have met her once—unless you are talking nonsense—you will definitely be amazed. Her face is painted as vividly as a rose, charming. Her two crystal-clear eyeballs are agile and flow like clear dewdrops on flower stamens. Her water chestnut-like lips seem to have been cut with a knife, quivering with blood-red color. Her eyebrows are painted as vividly and enchantingly as willow leaves. Her erect breasts, lightly wrinkled soft waist, and black hair are permed into a magical sparrow's nest. On her jade-like fingers, she wears a diamond ring worth a thousand gold. A pair of five- or six-inch-long fleshy feet are stuffed into high-heeled leather shoes that make a "de-de-de" sound when she walks. Other accessories, such as pearl earrings, a gold watch, a gold bracelet, and a platinum necklace... she has everything. She lives in a Western-style building, wears imported goods with constantly updated designs, and eats delicacies from the sea. Her daily work, besides drawing eyebrows, applying powder, putting on lipstick, perming her hair, spraying perfume, and manicuring her nails, is to chat and joke with her lover in the park, or whisper sweet nothings in front of champagne, reveling in self-satisfaction, or embrace and dance in the ballroom, or passionately kiss and indulge in the movie theater, or point fingers and gossip in the amusement park, or drive around in a car on the main street, showing off her thoroughly modern spirit. And then there are playing poker, mahjong, and gambling with dominoes and mahjong tiles.

As for her purpose in reading, it is to facilitate writing love letters, reading sexual histories, and looking at cosmetic advertisements and movie descriptions. The English that constantly flows from her mouth is "I Love you My Darling, Kiss Dancing Goal..." I ask you, what about Miss Wang is worthy of being called artistic? Alas!

In fact, aren't those women in Shanghai who live a life of pleasure and consider themselves modern all like Miss Wang, utterly ruined and filthy? I don't know the depths of Shanghai women's love for vanity!

[Amitabha]

— Wen Yuan

"Ding, ding, ding..." The doorbell kept ringing.

"Who is it? Mr. Ni is not at home." The servant A Er saw the two monks standing outside the door and answered before they could speak.

Because the guests at Wang's mansion were mostly wealthy merchants or high-ranking officials, what about the servants? They were usually very polite. But today, this low-class servant A Er spoke so arrogantly, which naturally surprised some people inside.

"Go and take a look outside. Has a mistress come?" Mama Wang, who liked to talk, said as she walked out.

"We are not here to beg for alms, but to see your madam. We have just come from Mount Emei in Sichuan and have brought some things to offer to you," the two monks explained their intentions and pushed the door with their hands.

"So it's these two great masters. Oh, it's been a long time! A Er, you're blind! Hurry up and open the door!" Mama Wang recognized the people and scolded A Er while specially walking down the stone steps to greet them.

These two guests entered the magnificent living room, sat on the sofa, put down the things wrapped in their hands, and chatted with Mama Wang.

"Oh, I forgot to invite the madam down."

Mama Wang talked for a long time before remembering to go upstairs to invite the hostess.

After a lot of small talk about Buddha, temples, and Fengdu City in Sichuan, etc., the younger of the two monks opened his bag and took out a stack of things wrapped in oil paper from the sutras.

"Madam, this is top-quality Yunnan soil. You can't buy it in Shanghai even if you have money. It's cheap in Sichuan. This package has a little less than fifty taels," the young monk uncovered the oil paper and handed it to the hostess to see.

"Good, very good." Mama Wang brought down the handbag from under the pillow upstairs. Madam Wang unfolded the thick stack of things with her hands, sniffed it with her nose, and then used her hands to test the weight.

"Here is one hundred and fifty yuan. You have worked hard. Please bring it again next time," Madam Wang took the money from her handbag and paid the monks.

"Amitabha!" The two monks took the money, clasped their hands together, and bowed to the ordinary female benefactor.

"Amitabha!" A Er opened the door for the monks and muttered to himself.

Live in a dream

Memories After Waking Up

— Dong Xin

There is one thing that gave me a very deep impression. Although the matter has passed, the situation of this event often appears in my mind, like scenes on a screen in a movie theater.

I remember one day last year, I was ordered by my father to buy something on Jing'an Temple Road. When I ran to the street, because it was raining, I jumped on a trolleybus on the Bund. When I stepped on the trolleybus, I couldn't help but mutter, "Brother Zhuo, I haven't seen you for a long time—" I was very happy at that time because I met a classmate I hadn't seen for a long time. Before I could finish my words, I felt surprised. Although he showed a happy expression on his face, his heart contained countless sorrows and pains.

I remember that he was in the same grade as me five years ago. Among the same grade, his age was considered the oldest. I also remember that he often wore very beautiful suits, his hair was combed very smoothly, and he applied a very thick layer of snow cream. He only attended classes two days a week, and the rest of the time he was out playing. Classmates all knew that he was the most romantic and richest person in the school. When he saw me at that time, he moved a little to make a seat for me. I felt that he was completely different from before, much thinner than before. He was only wearing a very old black cloth gown at that time, and I felt that his situation had undergone great changes. I asked him how he had been lately, he shook his head and sighed, and then began to say...

"Me? I think you know too. You see I am already different from before. I think you still remember. When I was your classmate before, how much the classmates envied me, thinking that my family had a large fortune. Ah, you definitely won't believe it when I say it, I really tell you, my mother used to work for people in the countryside." When he said this, his eyes couldn't help but turn red, and the tears in his eyes gradually swelled. I wanted to comfort him, but it was already too late. He sighed again and continued to say...

"But when I was in school, I often cheated the money my mother earned. Because I have no father and no siblings since I was young. So my mother often gave me money, and she did whatever I said. Therefore, she sent me to Shanghai to study, but I abandoned everything and didn't care at all, and went on the path of a prodigal son, violating the teachings of teachers and elders. Not to mention that I couldn't comfort my mother, but instead often wasted the money she earned with her blood and sweat, throwing it into the dark places. Ah, I am truly a great sinner, this really makes me regret and makes me sad.

But my mother passed away last year, and I feel pain in my life. Ah, how sinful I am!" After he finished speaking, tears kept flowing. In the end, I learned that he was working in a factory, with a monthly salary of only fifteen yuan. Jing'an Temple Road had arrived, so after I said goodbye to him, I couldn't help but shed a few tears of sympathy.

Car

A Melancholy Letter

— Si Zhong

Before picking up the pen, it seems that there are thousands of feelings to express, but when I pick up the pen, ah... where do I start?

"Life, ah, is originally a fleeting moment! The body, ah, is originally a drop in the ocean!" Whenever I think of this, how can I not think of "seizing the moment for pleasure" and enjoying the happiness of this golden age! But "the future is vast and worries are like the sea"! I can't help but feel sorrow.

Friend! Although I have not yet stepped into the path of society, although the demon of bread has not yet made things difficult for me. But ah! Several things have already proven my fate and can already make me dread the "path of life"!

Before, I remember having such a happy dream:

Page 18

"In a garden full of beautiful flowers, plants, and trees... the willow branches gently swayed her soft, slender waist, the snow-white ginkgo, the intoxicating magnolia, and the honeysuckle hidden deep in the vines were all smiling nimbly... but I only love the newly opened rose, because she has blush-like cheeks, because she has a fragrance that can refresh the heart. With such beautiful scenery, embellished with the clear sky, the warm sunshine, and the warbling yellow oriole that seems to be showing off its charm to me, a scene of "Heavenly Paradise" is completed." I just wander there, I just enjoy myself there, I just indulge myself there... all the roads presented before me are only bright, and everything that enters my eyes is happy!

However, this enchanting fantasy is not long-lasting! The beautiful garden is now desolate... the charming yellow oriole has flown elsewhere to show off... the sky is no longer as clear and lovely as before, only gloomy and bleak.

Whenever I think of everything in the future, melancholy thoughts ripple in my heart again, and crystal-like teardrops are about to burst out. Because I have no ability to revive this desolate garden, no ability to eradicate the thorns on the road, and even less ability to pursue light and create happiness!

Friend! When you see this letter, I guess you must be coming to advise me, saying... "Don't be negative, strive hard!" But, my dear friend! This is not necessary for me. Because I already know that decadence, depression, sadness, and worry can all hurt my heart and body and erode my life... but a dried-up lake can no longer ripple beautifully... a dead heart can no longer burn wildly.

When I write this, my hand is a little trembling, my limbs are just a trace of weakness, my eyes are full of crystalline tears, and something seems to be blocking my throat. I just want to cry loudly. If someone is willing to shed a tear of sympathy for me now, then I am truly grateful!

Friend! Please watch! Not many days from now, there will definitely be even more unpleasant news for you!

This melancholy letter can represent the thinking of the general youth of today. The fundamental mistake is to think of seizing the moment for pleasure and enjoying the happiness of this golden age. May I ask the certain gentleman who wrote the letter, is now the time for pleasure? Is it a golden age? Please let the general youth think about it. - Editor's note

Nonsense

Annotations of Student Slang

— Zhang Huijun

Pass: Cheating during exams.

Eating big dishes: Being questioned and punished by the school authorities for violating the rules.

Playing the pipa: Being flustered and confused when something happens.

La la team: The cheering squad at ball games.

Cheering: Female students attending ball games or joining the cheering squad, making the players excited.

L: L is the first letter of Love and the first letter of Letter, combined in a mathematical way to represent a love letter.

Palace: The female dormitory of a co-educational university is called the palace, such as the East Palace in Jiangwan and the West Palace in West Shanghai, to show respect. Male students entering the female dormitory are called entering the palace to pay respects.

Palace Lord: Since the female dormitory is called the palace, the female students are called the palace lord.

Empress: The most beautiful and sociable modern girl in a school, revered as the empress.

School Flower: The title of empress carries feudal ideas, so it is changed to the current name.

Changing clothes: Constantly changing fashions, even several sets a day.

Lemon Time: During ball game breaks, lemons are taken to quench thirst, so the break time is called lemon time.

Old master: A player who is not active.

Old gentleman: Someone who studies hard and doesn't like sports.

Little Kers

A Strange Society

— Lady Wuhuai

Since graduating from a certain school this year, driven by boredom and idleness, I have been thinking about finding something to do all day long. One day, I found an advertisement in the newspaper for a certain academic society hiring a clerk, and I resolutely decided to try it. But when reading the newspaper, I had a question, because since it is hiring a clerk, it should be based on elegant writing style, so why can't the works be seen, and only going to the interview counts? Later, because my curiosity was too strong, I went with a classmate.

This organization is located in an Apartment, and the office is only a small room. It lives on the top floor. When I knocked on the door, a young man came out to open the door and led me in. After writing my resume and salary, he said to me very gently, "Whether or not you are accepted, you will know in the next few days." At that time, I was very surprised and asked, "Sir, you have not seen my works, how can you judge your choice?"

He smiled and said, "Hiring a clerk does not necessarily require looking at the works. You only need to look at his face to know the keenness of this person's thoughts." I felt even stranger after hearing this, and secretly thought, can one's wisdom and knowledge be seen on the face? Then all the trials in society can be avoided, and a lot of trouble can be saved. The saying "clever face, stupid belly" should no longer exist, but he is an intellectual, maybe he won't lie.

I came out with my classmates in the midst of such full of doubts, and I still feel surprised until now. Alas, this is really a mysterious and strange society.
